Tokyo 300,000 People Mobilized for Air Defense Exercise Opens

Like London and Paris During the European War 28

)Tokyo( Japan's unprecedented air defense drill, centered on the capital and encompassing one prefecture and four counties as the stage, is fully prepared. It commenced with live ammunition bombing exercises on the coast of Chiba Prefecture on the 7th, which served as the opening salvo. From the 9th to the 11th, for a period of three days, it mobilized 300,000 people, including various units under its jurisdiction and veterans' and youth groups from the one prefecture and four counties, using "Protect Our Airspace" as its slogan and commencing action simultaneously. Dozens of aircraft participated in the drill, including fighter planes, reconnaissance planes, and light attack aircraft. The public's patriotic radio communications corps also participated. At 10:00 AM on the 9th, the Air Defense Command Headquarters at the Army Officer School issued the first report, "Enemy aircraft attacking, the capital is in imminent danger." Simultaneously, the Defense Commander ordered "Strive to defend" throughout the exercise area. As a result, the Kanto region entered a wartime state. At night, enemy air raids were simulated through electric lights, wireless telephones, sirens, and alarms. The capital was immediately placed under fire control, transforming into a dark world, resembling London and Paris during the European War. At the same time, bombing and smoke screens were demonstrated everywhere, along with various scientific combat exercises. The outcome of this drill is of great importance to Japan's national defense, and all parties are paying the utmost attention to its progress. )United Press International dispatch on the 6th(

The Japanese army, unable to gain international recognition for its aggression, believes that this antagonism cannot be resolved without a major war. Therefore, it daily intimidates the people with pronouncements that war is imminent, gradually transforming all organizations into wartime configurations, forcing the people to live under the threat of war. Recently, the Japanese people have indeed developed a kind of war neurosis, with a gloomy atmosphere pervading the country. The Tokyo Garrison Command decided to conduct a large-scale Kanto air defense drill for three days starting August 9th. The detailed plan is as follows:

The United States as the Enemy in Strategy 29

The Opponent in Air Defense

Is the United States. It is assumed that diplomatic relations with the United States were severed on August 1st, and war was declared simultaneously. The Japanese and American navies have already opened fire at sea. An American aircraft carrier has arrived at the Ogasawara Islands, advancing straight towards Kanto Bay, ordering its air force to bomb Tokyo City. The Japanese army received a report from the navy and immediately ordered the Tokyo Garrison Command to prepare for air defense, simultaneously announcing defense orders for the one prefecture and four counties. Commander Hayashi, upon receiving the order, immediately established an Air Defense Command Headquarters at the Army Officer School, announced a wartime organization, deployed the planned air defense forces, and commenced operations. Communication units, surveillance units, anti-aircraft artillery units, illumination units, sound detection units, guard units, medical units, liaison units, and fire brigades were all mobilized simultaneously.

Air Force Strengths of Both Sides 30

In This Exercise, the

Air force strengths of both sides are as follows: The US Navy dispatched fifty ship-based fighter planes and bombers from aircraft carriers, flying from the southeast sea to bomb the imperial capital and various important cities (if the weather is bad, army aircraft from Otawara will be used instead). The Japanese air defense flying squadron will respond with the latest army fighter planes, with the strength of three squadrons, dispatched from Tokorozawa and Tachikawa, ambushing at predetermined locations, awaiting orders.

Japanese Air Defense Deployment 31

This Large-Scale

Air defense drill is centered on Tokyo City, with a population of five million, with the surrounding four prefectures serving as air defense zones, divided into six zones: the Tokyo Zone, the Kanagawa Zone, the Yokosuka Naval Port Zone, the Chiba Zone, the Ibaraki Zone, and the Saitama Zone. The vast area, with a radius of 150 kilometers and a diameter of 300 kilometers, includes the four major cities of Tokyo, Yokohama, Kawasaki, and Yokosuka. The participating army and navy units are as follows: 1. Tokyo Garrison Command; 2. Infantry, field artillery, and communication units of the Konoe Division; 3. Infantry and heavy artillery units of the 1st Division; 4. Field artillery and anti-aircraft artillery units of the 3rd Division; 5. Field artillery and heavy artillery units of the 4th Division; 6. Heavy artillery units of the 7th Division; 7. Mountain artillery units of the 9th Division; 8. Mountain artillery units of the 11th Division; 9. Infantry and engineer units of the 14th Division; 10. Field artillery and heavy artillery units of the 16th Division; 11. Army Field Artillery School; 12. Army Automotive School; 13. Aircraft carriers and aircraft units belonging to the Yokosuka Naval District; 14. Officials from various government agencies, such as the Tokyo Prefecture, Kanagawa Prefecture, Chiba Prefecture, Saitama Prefecture, Ibaraki Prefecture, the Metropolitan Police Department, the Ministry of Communications, the Tokyo Railway Bureau, the Tokyo Communications Bureau, and the authorities of the four cities; 15. The Central Radio Broadcasting Station; 16. Workers from civilian companies and factories.

The navy attacks, the army defends. The deployment of various air defense units is centered on the Imperial Palace, with a radius of 150 kilometers. The actual situation of the deployment is as follows: 1. Anti-aircraft artillery and various artillery units and balloon units are deployed within 20 kilometers; 2. Sound detection units are set up within 40 kilometers; 3. Illumination units and fighter aircraft units are set up within 70 kilometers; 4. Radio forward communication units and observation posts are set up in the area within 100 to 150 kilometers; 5. 300,000 citizens participating in the civil defense corps.

Currently, the Tokyo city area is organized into the Imperial Capital Defense Corps, with a total of 35 groups and 300,000 personnel. Youth groups, veterans, and virgin societies from various places are also ordered to participate. The Tokyo Garrison Command issued a notice to the citizens in the war zone, requiring each to prepare their own protective equipment and demonstrating air defense methods as follows: 1. Each household must set up a gas-proof room and enter this room to avoid gas attacks upon receiving an alarm; 2. Do not panic or rush, remain calm, and act according to the instructions; 3. Pay attention to security at all times; 4. After hearing the alarm, do not loiter outdoors, immediately enter the nearby houses for shelter or enter the government-established shelters; 5. If there are no houses nearby, enter the roadside ditches for shelter; 6. Be vigilant against fires; 7. The safest place in the house is next to the hard walls, do not approach the windows. Criticism from Relevant Parties 33

Guarantee the import of a certain quantity of Indian cotton every year. The intention is to reduce the tariffs on Indian cotton cloth as a concession. However, the agriculture and forestry and commerce and industry authorities strongly opposed matters under their jurisdiction. British Naval Department's Shipbuilding Plan

Catching Up with the US and Japan, US International Policy Changes )London( It is recently heard that the British Naval Department is currently planning to enrich the navy by increasing the number of cruisers, destroyers, and submarines. This expenditure will be included in the budget for approximately the next year. However, it is not intended to be built before 1936, because these new ships are completely outside the limits of the London Treaty. The reason for this move by the British is caused by the shipbuilding programs of the United States and Japan. Although the ships built by the two countries are within the scope of the treaty, their urgent activities to expand their navies show that there have been changes in policies on reducing armaments. Therefore, the British are also catching up. (National News Agency dispatch on the 6th)

(Washington) Today, the US State Department formally denied that Japan had protested against the US shipbuilding program. At the same time, officialdom also indicated that the US government has temporarily abandoned the so-called "outward-looking" policy and will no longer initiate any international movements. However, for those initiated by other countries, if they do not have major conflicts with the current revival plan of nationalism, they are still prepared to cooperate. According to widespread rumors in London, Japan is quite anxious about the US shipbuilding policy and has protested to the United States that it does not conform to the spirit of the Washington and London treaties. Therefore, the US State Department specifically denied today that the United States does not violate the treaty, even if the new ships are built, they still do not exceed the treaty limits. At the same time, according to sources outside the State Department, the US government's strong rejection of the proposal to stabilize currency prices at the World Economic Conference is the beginning of adopting a "looking after oneself" policy. It has been over a decade since the United States actively participated in international affairs, advocating new treaties, new economic cooperation, and other cooperative actions. This rejection of stabilizing currency and the start of the naval program, declaring that the US Navy must not be inferior to other countries, can all be regarded as the beginning of its nationalist plan. However, it is also solemnly stated that the US President does not approve of opening up an isolationist policy. After taking office, he tried to continue Hoover's international policy, the so-called "Stimson Doctrine," which he also supported. However, in the near future, there may be very little advice to other countries, and even on the issue of disarmament, this policy will be followed. In Geneva in the future, there will probably only be suggestions, or there will no longer be sharp applications and requests. Although the policy previously pursued by the United States will not be abandoned, it will no longer launch new international events. (National News Agency dispatch on the 6th)

Reuters Rome dispatch on the 5th. The German National Socialist Party used radio broadcasts to conduct propaganda in Austria and used airplanes to drop leaflets in Austria. France and Britain have sent documents to negotiate with the German government. Italy was initially expected to join this action, but today, according to a certain official from the Italian Ministry of Foreign Affairs, Italy is now being cautious and it is inconvenient to join and there is no need to join. However, according to non-official sources, Italian Prime Minister Mussolini is very concerned about this matter and has informally reiterated his advice in Berlin in a gentle state. The wording is very euphemistic. According to news from Paris, the notes from Britain and France to Germany are very euphemistic. However, the right-wing opposition party still thinks that the methods used are too weak, while the Socialist Party believes that this matter should be transferred to the League of Nations for handling. The moderates do not want to punish Germany and also hope that the determination of British-French cooperation can make Austrian sovereignty respected.

Havas Berlin dispatch on the 6th. Regarding the German National Socialist Party using airplanes to distribute leaflets in Austria, Reuters reported that the British government has instructed its ambassador to Berlin to negotiate with the German government, and France and Italy seem to have joined this action. However, according to reliable sources on the other hand, it seems that this

Negotiations have not yet been proposed, and it is expected to be realized on Monday. Havas Vienna dispatch on the 5th. The newspapers here all published news that the Austrian National Socialist Party, which is hiding in Sengcheng, Germany, has drafted a list of the Austrian National Socialist Party cabinet and will replace Dollfuss. The newspapers publishing this list also stated that the proposed cabinet of the Austrian National Socialist Party will be headed by Prokesch, the leader of the Austrian National Socialist Party who is currently in Sengcheng. The Austrian police authorities corrected this news, saying that it was a brief list found by the police in Linz, Austria. The police continued to eliminate the National Socialist Party movement and also discovered a secret propaganda agency of the Hitler Party in Vienna, seizing secret code documents, including letters to and from the foreign affairs office of the German Hitler Party. In addition, a German was arrested in Langenzerdorf, Austria, and secret code letters were seized, which were used to communicate with Germany.

Roosevelt Vigorously Implements Labor-Management Truce 58

Issues Emergency Application to the Entire US Industry to Set Up an Arbitration Board to Mediate Labor-Management Disputes National News Agency Hyde Park dispatch on the 5th. US President Roosevelt issued an emergency application to the national industry today, requesting to stop all means of strikes and factory closures, gather all sectors of the country, and promote the industrial recovery plan to ensure its early success. The US President issued this application after hearing the news that the coal miners, after mediation by the Miners' Union Chairman Lewis and other labor leaders, agreed to resume work and work according to the mining industry's industry rules sent to the President, and hoping that all sectors will immediately accept the advice, a arbitration board was specially established to mediate all labor-management disputes, commissioning General Electric Company Chairman Stewart, American Federation of Labor Chairman Green and Senator Wagner as arbitrators, and requesting the capital side to permanently abandon the means of closing factories when workers request increased wages or improved treatment, and at the same time requesting workers not to strike and send their requests to the arbitration board. The organization of the arbitration board will follow the regulations of the arbitration board that arbitrated wage disputes in factories manufacturing military supplies during the European War. At that time, the late President Taft served as the director of the board, and all disputes could be resolved to the satisfaction of both parties. However, President Roosevelt's arbitration board this time is quite inclined to the labor side, and even the capital side representative Stewart is the leader of the great movement to enable all the unemployed to get jobs and receive fair wages. Senator Wagner, who is the proposer of the unemployment relief plan, has always been a great protector of the labor community, and this time he also accompanied other labor officials and large industrialists to ask the President to find a way to prevent strikes. However, the US President is personally responsible for the actions of the arbitration board and will not make a final decision without his consideration.

50,000 Miners Still on Strike 59

National News Agency Enxing Town (Pennsylvania) dispatch on the 6th. 50,000 striking coal miners voted today to continue the strike and will not resume work on Monday. According to the advice of labor-management truce given by US President and Industrial Recovery Director Johnson, and the news that workers may accept the proposals of the arbitration board, this resolution was quite unexpected to the general public.

The Situation in Cuba is Grave 60

A Nationwide General Strike Serves as a Prelude to Open Revolution

Havana, 5th (Special Dispatch): A general strike continues in Cuba today. It is widely rumored that striking workers and revolutionaries in the interior have clashed with the military and police in numerous incidents, but this has not yet been verified here. This is because telegraph personnel are also on strike, resulting in a communication breakdown. However, there have also been conflicts in the capital, injuring many people. It is anticipated that casualties have also occurred in the provinces. The strikers are now openly demanding the resignation of President Machado and the restoration of constitutional rights, which were suspended by Machado about two years ago due to political unrest. Machado remains concerned and has not yet declared martial law. He met with advisors today to discuss the situation. Many expect the strike to be a prelude to open revolution, with uprisings likely to occur in the capital and provinces in the coming days.

Poland and Danzig Conclude Port Affairs Agreement 61

Of Great Importance to Peace in Eastern Europe

Warsaw, 5th (Reuters): Representatives of the Polish government and the Danzig National Socialist government have recently negotiated the utilization of the port of Danzig and concluded an agreement, which was signed today. This agreement is of great importance to peace in Eastern Europe. The port of Danzig has suffered in recent years due to competition from the nearby Polish port of Gdynia. The agreement establishes a foundation aimed at ensuring that Danzig also benefits from Poland's maritime development.

Warsaw, 5th (Havas): Poland and the Free City of Danzig have negotiated an agreement on the rights of Polish people and the minority Polish population residing in the Free City, which was signed today in Danzig. In addition, Poland has also reached an agreement on the utilization of the Free Port of Danzig, with its terms also approved by both parties. According to this agreement, Poland will participate in the port of Danzig to promote maritime development.

Brownshirt Party Military Parade 64

With a Participation of 180,000

Berlin, 6th (Havas): The National Socialist Party's Brownshirt military held a large-scale parade at the former Doeberitz military training ground, with a participation of 180,000 people. They were selected purely from the party military in Berlin and Brandenburg and inspected by Chief of Staff of the Party Military, Major Roehm. Roehm rode on horseback, flanked by other officers. When the National Socialist Party military was first established, it fought for revolution, and they were inspected while arranged in small groups. This time, the arrangement was almost identical to a real national army, with troop units equivalent to regiments and brigades of a formal army. During the march, they were led by an honorary banner, with two escort teams of approximately sixty people flanking it, all wearing brown shirts, steel helmets, and shouldering rifles, led by an officer holding a saber. Spectator seats required admission fees, so only 10,000 people attended, with few ordinary citizens. Most were petty-bourgeois officers, government officials, diplomatic corps representatives, and foreign National Socialists.

Poland Revises Constitution 65

Warsaw, 6th (Havas): The Parliamentary Government Party held a large-scale meeting, where leader Sławek expressed his opinion advocating for a major revision of the Polish Constitution. The current Government Party holds a majority in Parliament, so the proposed constitutional revision will certainly pass. The aim of this reform is to enhance the authority of the President and place citizens in a merely "passive and defensive" position in politics. The President may issue legislative decrees at any time to govern the country. Another aim of the reform is to reorganize the Senate and enhance its power. The Senate has historically been elected by universal suffrage. According to the reform proposal, one-third of the senators will be appointed by the President, and two-thirds will be elected by a special electoral body. The new Senate will enjoy equal rights with the House of Representatives, so even if the opposition faction gradually gains importance in the House of Representatives, the government can still control the parliamentary situation.

Belgium and Soviet Russia Negotiate Resumption of Relations Successfully 66

Brussels, 6th (National Dispatch): Negotiations between Belgium and Soviet Russia regarding the resumption of diplomatic relations are progressing smoothly, with significant progress. It is said that this is the result of the recent visit here by the Soviet Russian Ambassador to France.

French Aviators Attempt to Fly Across the Atlantic 67

Competing for the Longest Distance Straight Line Flight Record

Paris, 6th (Havas): French aviators Rossi and Codos departed from New York yesterday morning at 5:00 AM in an attempt to fly across the Atlantic and break the world record for the longest straight-line flight. The two pilots transmitted messages via radio, reporting their flight conditions. The Ministry of Aviation received and published the reports. One message stated, "This morning at 9:00 AM (Greenwich Mean Time), we were unable to send a report due to severe weather conditions at sea, making the flight difficult." Shortly after, another message stated, "We are battling a low-pressure system over Halifax, Canada, and it has been very difficult to cope with for five hours." At 9:45 AM, the Ministry of Aviation issued the following radio message: "We have now flown to a point approximately 1,000 kilometers from the British coast and the Isles of Scilly." Furthermore, the American mail ship Manhattan in the Atlantic received radio messages from three other ships at 9:45 AM (Greenwich Mean Time), stating that they had intercepted reports from Codos and Rossi that they had flown to a point 600 kilometers from the coast of England. Therefore, the first step of Codos and Rossi's plan has been successful.

London, 6th (Havas): At 1:50 PM, the Saint-Just radio station received a radio message from Codos and Rossi stating that they had flown to a point 200 miles west of "Cape Race."

Song Zheyuan Goes to Shuisha City Via Jin 68

)The Peaceful Resolution of the Chahar Situation Is Nearing Success(

(Special Dispatch from Beiping) After efforts by various parties to mediate a peaceful resolution, there is hope for the Chahar political situation, which has dragged on for more than two months. Song Zheyuan, Chairman of Chahar Province, accompanied by Xiong Bin, Jiang Bocheng, Qin Dechun, and others, departed for Shacheng this morning (5th) at 7:45 AM, arriving around 1:00 PM. Feng Yuxiang also sent Tong Lin'ge to Shacheng at the same time to meet with Song and discuss solutions. It is said that Song will return to Beiping on the 6th. Feng will wait for Tong Lin'ge to return to Zhangjiakou and report on the meeting with Song before telegraphing on the 6th to cancel the name of the Anti-Japanese Allied Army. As for Feng's personal title, he has already stated that it is not an issue. Therefore, after the telegraph, he only hopes to have the freedom to reside where he pleases. Song Zheyuan will handle the Chahar situation. In general, the troops of Ji Hongchang, Sun Liangcheng, and Tong Lin'ge will all be reorganized into divisions and brigades, respectively. The various volunteer armies will retain their original designations. Fang Zhenwu's army only has the two units of Bao Gang and Zhang Renjie. Bao's unit has already been reorganized into the 45th Brigade by the Military Affairs Committee. Zhang's unit will also be reorganized, so there are no significant issues. However, Fang personally requested to be appointed as the Border Defense Commissioner of Chahar Province. The authorities here still hope that he will leave the military and be given a civilian position. This still needs further discussion.

Since Deng Zhexiyi brought Feng Yuxiang's telegraph on July 31st to Beiping and reported it to the authorities, there has been a turning point in the Chahar situation. He Yingqin then proposed three measures on the 3rd, telegraphing Feng to solicit his opinion. After receiving the telegram, Feng, in addition to issuing a winter telegram accepting the four principles of Jiang and Wang's telegraph, also sent Liu Zhizhou and Wang Menqing to Shacheng on the 3rd to visit Pang Bingxun, conveying Feng's letter stating that he could accept the three measures proposed by He and that he would cease military activities from the 4th, and welcome Chairman Song to return to Chahar, first restoring smooth traffic. Pang reported the situation to He Yingqin, who then summoned Qin Dechun and Xiong Bin to Jurentang on the morning of the 4th to discuss everything. He then invited Song Zheyuan to inform him that Feng welcomed him to return to office and requested him to make a final effort for Chahar and make a trip to Shacheng in order to achieve success. At the same time, Song also received telegrams from various parties urging him, stating that if the Chahar situation was prolonged for too long, it would be detrimental to the country and to himself, and that he must find a way to resolve it. Song then agreed to make the trip, and He issued an order, ordering Song to enter Shacheng, adhering to the government's intention to handle everything. After Song excused himself, he invited Deng Zhexiyi, Qin Dechun, Xiong Bin, and others at 5:00 PM for further discussions. At the same time, Feng appropriately sent a telegram to Song welcoming him, saying that he would send Tong Lin'ge to Shacheng to meet with him, hoping to indicate the time of departure. Ji Hongchang, Tong Lin'ge, and others also telegraphed Song to welcome him. Song then decided to depart for Shacheng on the morning of the 5th, and a special train and a battalion of guards were transferred to the Xizhimen Station for standby.

After the itinerary was decided, He sent Xiong Bin and Jiang Bocheng as representatives to accompany him. Xiong's eye disease had not yet fully recovered, so he also made an effort to go. On the morning of the 5th, at around 6:00 AM, Song, Qin, Deng, and others spoke briefly, and then dispersed. At around 7:00 AM, Jiang Bocheng, Xiong Bin, Deng Zhexiyi, Chen Xiwen, Yang Zhennan, and others arrived at Xizhimen Station one after another. Finally, Song arrived at the station with Qin Dechun, exchanged greetings with the welcomers Men Zhizhong, He Yingqin's representative Xu Ying, and Liu Shifu, and then boarded the train. At 7:45 AM, the train departed. Before Song left Beiping, he met with visitors at the station and said that the Chahar situation had been delayed for more than two months, and the central government had consistently determined to handle it peacefully, and Chairman He was also proceeding with this goal. Recently, Mr. Feng expressed his willingness to make peace. After all, bullets belong to the country, and each one fired is one more loss. I was unable to exert myself fully due to a recurrence of my lower back pain, and I am deeply ashamed. Recently, because all parties are willing to make peace, and I received an order from the Military Affairs Committee Branch, I decided to go to Shacheng. After arriving, I will telegraph Zhangjiakou, asking Mr. Feng to send two representatives to Shacheng to discuss everything. I expect that after this negotiation, the Chahar problem can be resolved. (August 5th)

Huang Fu Passes Through Hankou to Xunyang 69

)To Ask Jiang for Instructions on Handling the North China Situation(

(Zhang Qun Accompanies Him to Report on the Political Situation in Hubei Province) Hankou Correspondence: Huang Fu, Chairman of the Beiping Political Affairs Committee, was summoned south by Chairman Chiang Kai-shek. He handed over the affairs of the Political Affairs Committee to Secretary-General He Qigong to handle on his behalf. He traveled south by special train from Beiping on the evening of the 3rd, accompanied only by Secretaries He and Guo, and one attendant. The train passed through Zhengzhou on the 4th, arriving in Hankou at 1:25 PM on the 5th. Many military and political figures from Wuhan went to welcome him. After Huang disembarked, he went to the General Headquarters' office in Hankou to rest and met with Cao Haosen, He Chengjun, Zhang Qun, and others. At 9:00 PM that evening, he took the Jiang'an steamer to Xunyang. Zhang Qun also traveled east on the same boat to report to Chiang on the political situation in Hubei Province. It is estimated that they will arrive in Xunyang on the morning of the 6th and ascend Guling in the afternoon. Huang made a statement in Hankou, briefly stating that the North China Political Affairs Committee had been established for more than two months. During this period, it has been handling urgent and extraordinary affairs. When an event occurs, a decision must be made within three minutes and resolved within ten minutes, because delay may cause changes. The takeover of the war zone has now been completed in seventeen counties. Only Miyun and Zunhua have not yet been taken over, and it will be completed in three or four days. For post-war reconstruction in the war zone, the central government has decided to allocate 1 million yuan in cash and issue 4 million yuan in public bonds for relief efforts. It has been decided to use 2 million yuan for emergency relief and 3 million yuan for agricultural relief. War zone refugees are displaced, miserable, and starving. Emergency relief must first be used to maintain life, and the fundamental relief must be to restore the countryside and stabilize people's lives. Recalling the time of the war, homes in various places were destroyed by artillery fire, and plows and agricultural tools were looted. Therefore, agricultural relief must be implemented, and loans must be given to the people so that they can purchase all necessary tools for farming. However, the area of the Luan River East war zone is more than forty times larger than the Shanghai war zone, and the suffering of the people is even greater than in Shanghai. Therefore, the funds raised are far from sufficient. It is hoped that compatriots across the country will show their sympathy and donate as much as possible so that the survivors of the looting can recover. The Chahar incident has been happening for a long time, and there has been no result from the envoys going back and forth. The crux of the matter is that Feng and Fang must discuss military and political affairs together and resolve them at the same time. The central government must first cancel their titles and then discuss political issues. Judging from the current situation, there is no danger of an unfortunate event occurring, but I fear that prolonging it for too long will affect foreign relations, and the more disputes there will be. At this time of national crisis, all citizens should thoroughly awaken and work together harmoniously. The Political Affairs Committee will only adhere to the central government's intention to seek a solution through peaceful means for the Chahar situation. As for the suspension of traffic on the Beiping-Suiyuan Railway, it is because Feng and Fang withdrew road funds and detained vehicles. However, traffic from Beiping to Xiahuayuan and from Suiyuan to Chaigoubao is still normal. The traffic on that road has not been completely cut off. In addition, reports say that the Japanese authorities dispatched the Third Fleet Commander Mineichi, who sailed to North China on the flagship Tenryu on the 2nd with the 27th Destroyer Division, suggesting some kind of action. There is no basis for this. I am going to Ganzhou tonight to meet Chiang Kai-shek and report on the situation in North China and discuss the future policy for handling political affairs. Whether I go to Nanjing or not will depend on meeting Chiang Kai-shek. (August 5th)

Jiangxi Province Establishes Four Political Bureaus in Bandit Areas 70

)Longgang, Tengtian, Fenggang, and Xinfeng( )Using Political Power to Assist in Bandit Suppression(

Nanchang Correspondence: Various Red bandit groups, such as Fang Zhimin in Mount Mopan, Zhu Xianzhi in Yuanlian, and Wang Zuo and Yuan Wencai in Jinggang, all started with only a few broken rifles in poor and remote areas where political power could not reach. Previously, Chairman Chiang Kai-shek convened a five-province bandit suppression conference in Nanchang, and the 50th Division proposed to establish county-level and assistant administrative organs in counties with vast territories and adjacent areas where the whip of authority could not reach. This was approved and handed over to the four departments of the headquarters for handling. Now, Director Zhu has determined that political power is often lacking in the Tengtian, Longgang, Fenggang, and Xinfeng areas of southeastern Jiangxi. Therefore, the above four places have been designated as special districts, with a political bureau established in each district, hoping to use political power to assist in bandit suppression. This measure has been approved by Chairman Chiang Kai-shek, who instructed the provincial government to demarcate the boundaries and prepare budget estimates for implementation. The plan is as follows: ㈠ Tengtian: located in the south of Yongfeng, including the fifth, sixth, and seventh districts of Yongfeng, the second district of Le'an, and the third and eighth districts of Gaoshui. ㈡ Fenggang: located in the east of Chongren, formerly the main base of Zhu and Mao's army in the upper reaches of the Fu River, now just recovered, including the fifth and seventh districts of Chongren and the second and third districts of Yihuang. ㈢ Xinfeng: located in the far south of Yihuang, bordering Nanfeng, Le'an, and Ningdu, formerly also one of the bandit strongholds, now the bandits have withdrawn, including the seventh district of Nanfeng, the fifth district of Yihuang, and the northern district of Ningdu adjacent to Kuzhu. ㈣ Longgang: located in the area bordering Yongfeng, Jishui, Ji'an, Taihe, Xingguo, Ningdu, and Le'an, formerly a stronghold equal to Donggu and Zhaoxie, an important base of Zhu and Mao. In 1932, it was included in Pingchi County, which was changed from Donggu, but later Donggu was abandoned, and Longgang became uncivilized again. This time, the eighth district of Yongfeng, the seventh district of Jishui, and the seventh district of Ji'an are re-suppressed. Each of the above four political bureaus has an annual expenditure of 22,584 yuan to handle the recruitment of refugees, the resettlement of coerced individuals, assisting the military in blockading the bandit areas, constructing defensive works, organizing baojia teams, building roads, and handling local personnel disputes, in order to clarify the source of bandits and restore order. However, before the establishment of the Northern Route Headquarters, it is handled by the Central Route Army Headquarters. Chen Cheng, Commander of the Central Route Army, has consulted the provincial government for the appointment of the heads of the four bureaus, which will be established immediately.

In addition, Ninggang County, which was captured for five years, has recently been recovered by the Hunan Army. The county town is desolate and broken, with less than a hundred families, and it is extremely difficult to restore. The county magistrate, Wang Shaoqi, has been approved to move the county town to Longshi, which is conveniently located for transportation between Hunan and Jiangxi.

Soldiers in Shenyang Make a Big Scene at the Theater 71

)Six or Seventy Fake Soldiers Wanted to Enter Without Buying Tickets, Shot and Killed Three Actors and Two Vendors(

(Special Dispatch from Diantong, Shenyang, 6th) The Futian Opera Troupe was performing at the Xiaohuayuan outside Dadongmen in Shenyang. Suddenly, on the afternoon of the 5th, sixty or seventy soldiers of "Manchukuo" wanted to enter the theater without buying tickets, and were refused by the theater owner. They then began to riot and fight. During the chaos, the soldiers suddenly opened fire, causing great chaos. Spectators fled in panic. As a result, three actors and two vendors were killed, and two vendors were seriously injured. The military police patrols heard the alarm and mobilized to suppress the incident. Wuxi.

Cracking Down on Counterfeit Champagne Ticket Organization 72

Manager Lu of the Shanghai Times branch in Qingguoxiang, Wuxi, in addition to selling newspapers, also sold various lottery tickets, making a considerable profit. Recently, a woman named Lu Huifen purchased a Dingzhi Qingdao Grand Champagne ticket for ten yuan. Huifen did not notice it at the time, but the real Grand Champagne ticket was originally scheduled to be drawn on the 30th of last month. However, because it was the same date as the Aviation Highway Construction Lottery, the Qingdao General Office announced that it would be postponed. Lu did not know about the postponement and sent the fake number list to Lu Huifen as scheduled. After receiving it, Huifen became suspicious, wondering why a number list would be sent when the newspaper had just announced a postponement. She then wrote to the Qingdao General Office to inquire. After receiving the letter, the office immediately wrote to the Minghua Bank on Beijing Road, Shanghai, the manager of the lottery, asking them to investigate. The bank then sent employees Xu Yongsheng and Qiu Yulin to Wuxi. At around 10:00 AM yesterday, they went to the Times branch in Qingguoxiang and pretended to check the numbers. Sure enough, Lu Juyi took out a fake number list. Therefore, they immediately called the police and took Lu Juyi and the fake number list and fake Champagne tickets to the First Public Security Bureau, and presented them to the County Public Security Bureau. Chief Wu opened a court and interrogated him. Lu Juyi was ordered to be detained pending transfer to the County Court for interrogation.

Rickshaw Pullers on General Strike 73

There are more than 50 rickshaw companies in the county, and 30 or 40 independent pullers who are not members of the union. There are a total of 2,214 rickshaws in the county. Before September of last year, the daily rental per rickshaw was four jiao of small coins and two copper coins. For rickshaws operating in Kaiyuan and Yangming townships, an additional 24 copper coins were charged. Rickshaws operating solely in the Wuxi urban area did not pay extra rent. The rickshaw owners, recognizing that the inability of rickshaws to operate uniformly in urban and rural areas greatly affected their business, decided to allow rickshaws to operate uniformly in urban and rural areas without boundaries starting on September 1st of last year. Since the unification, passengers have found it more convenient, and it was agreed that the daily rental per rickshaw would be three jiao and seven fen, equivalent to 1,380 copper coins. However, since the uniform operation and the lowering of rental prices, the economy has been in a state of panic, and business has been slow. Only 50% to 60% of rickshaws were rented out. Therefore, the smallest rickshaw companies secretly reduced rental prices to maintain their livelihoods, ranging from 600 to 800 to 1,040 copper coins per rickshaw. However, the majority of these rickshaws were old and dilapidated. Over time, most rickshaw companies also secretly reduced prices, destroying the agreement. If they did not reduce prices, no one would rent their rickshaws, so they had to comply outwardly but defy inwardly. Until recently, the silk factories in the county successively resumed operations, and commerce began to turn around. The economy gradually improved, and the number of rickshaws rented out increased daily. The rickshaw owners, realizing that they had been losing money for almost a year, convened a general membership meeting at the end of last month to discuss reorganizing rental prices. From August 6th, they would uniformly restore the price to three jiao and seven fen, and notified each rickshaw company in advance. After receiving the notice, each rickshaw company naturally informed the rickshaw pullers. The rickshaw pullers who were paying 1,040 copper coins per day did not have a problem, but the rickshaw pullers who were paying 500 to 600 copper coins per day felt greatly aggrieved and expressed their opposition, saying that the price had suddenly doubled. However, they had no organization. Yesterday (6th), after dawn, the majority of good rickshaw pullers still went to the companies to rent rickshaws. A group of rickshaw pullers who made a living by "selling shifts" went out to cause trouble. More than 100 rickshaw pullers gathered outside Guangfu Gate. The rest gathered at Yinglong Bridge outside the West Gate, and some even smashed the rickshaws on the road. Seeing this, the rickshaw pullers returned the rickshaws to their companies. In an instant, all rickshaws disappeared from the streets, and a general strike was carried out. County Magistrate Yan Shenyu received a report from the trade association the day before, requesting him to instruct the County Public Security Bureau to prevent the rickshaw pullers from taking extrajudicial actions. Yesterday morning, County Magistrate Yan received a report of the rickshaw pullers' strike and the gathering of rickshaw pullers outside Guangfu Gate and other places. He immediately telephoned the County Public Security Bureau and the County Investigation Brigade to dispatch armed police teams to various places to persuade them to return and ordered the rickshaw pullers to disperse. Because they had no unity, the rickshaw pullers gradually dispersed and waited for a solution. County Magistrate Yan instructed Technical Director Zhang Fulin and Zhao Xuchang, Xu Xingqiao, and Wang Zhiming, standing committee members of the rickshaw industry association preparatory committee, to come to the county office to discuss the reasons for the price increase. Zhao Xuchang and others presented everything in person, saying that the restoration of the original price was decided by a general membership meeting and that the matter could only be resolved by convening a general meeting to discuss solutions. They agreed to convene a temporary membership meeting at 5:00 PM to discuss solutions and immediately took their leave. However, the county government believed that the procedure was improper and that they should have reported to the county government and issued a notice in advance, and then this problem would not have occurred. The rickshaw owners were determined to achieve a rental price of three jiao and seven fen per rickshaw per day. Starting from that day, only 70% of the rickshaws would be released, and the remaining 30% of the licenses would be deposited in the trade association to prevent compliance outwardly but defiance inwardly. The remaining 30% of the old and dilapidated rickshaws would be repaired. All monthly licenses and monthly donations would still be paid as before. For this reason, the rickshaw rental price could not be reduced any further. The County Chamber of Commerce also paid close attention to this matter and encouraged the rickshaw owners to make slight concessions to resolve the matter immediately and avoid accidents, and asked County Magistrate Yan to instruct them to pay attention to local security. By noon, there were no rickshaw pullers on the streets, so order was as usual. Whether the rickshaw pullers can resume work immediately depends on whether the rickshaw owners can make concessions.

Nantong and Huainan Salt Lands Demarcated for Tilling 74

The Ministry of Finance believes that the salt lands of Huainan have not been reorganized to this day. In order to meet the actual situation, they are demarcating for tilling, and have decided to return them to the people and the salt farmers. Starting this month, they will begin surveying, starting from Jinsha in Nantong and progressing north, passing through Rugao, Dongtai, Xinghua, Yancheng, and finally Funing. Li Jing, the inspector of salt lands in Huainan and the captain of the survey team, has arrived in Nantong with the surveyors.

The maritime patrol team stationed along the coast of Tonghai and the Yangtze River was originally under the jurisdiction of the Yangtze River Water Police Bureau. Now that the Water Police Bureau has been abolished, the team has also been ordered to disband.

Jiangyin Land and Water Police Teams Divide Up Opium 76

On the night of July 22nd, the County Police First Detachment and the Water Police 20th Detachment discovered smuggled opium in Old Sea of Shazhou. Only 500 taels were delivered to the county. After someone reported to the county that the land and water police teams were dividing it up, they presented a detailed list to the county and filed a complaint with the Civil Affairs Department. The total amount of opium seized was over 3,000 taels. Boatmen Wang Xiaolao and Song Lao received over 1,500 taels each. After selling off more than 1,000 taels, over 2,000 taels were seized by the police teams and divided. The police first detachment leader, Min Wei, received 100 taels. The water police first detachment patrol officers, Chen Yanyi and Yuan Haichou, received 180 taels each. The informant, Sun Jinhuan, received 80 taels. Sun Yongnian received 50 taels. Zhang Zhong received 41 taels. Huang Luoshu, Fan Jizhi, Lu Jieshan, Tian Hengde, and a Zhao woman received 30 taels each. Zhou Desheng received 20 taels. Yin Huirong received 15 taels. Local thugs received 5 taels each. The police team soldiers received 10.5 taels each for 20 men. The squad leaders received 22 taels. The water police patrolmen received 10.5 taels each for 20 men. After receiving the report, County Magistrate Ruan has already put the boatmen in custody for interrogation.

Hardships of Life Lead to Suicide by Drowning 77

Zhou Hansheng, also known as Zhuge Shaolun, a resident of North Waiheng Street, was thirty-eight years old. He was married to a woman named Zhu and had three sons, the eldest being eleven and the youngest five. He used to work at the Licheng Wheel Bureau in Wuxi, but during the Dragon Boat Festival this year, the bureau's manager, Zhang Jianmen, laid off Zhou due to poor business. After being laid off, Zhou found it difficult to make ends meet at home and recently contracted malaria. As a result, he felt increasingly unable to cope and developed a desire to end his life. He went to the West Outer City River yesterday (the 5th) at around 3:00 PM and drowned himself.

Business Tax Collection Begins in Zhenjiang and Zhenyang 78

The business tax in Jiangsu Province has been under reorganization since the autumn of last year, and it has been a year now. However, the actual revenue collected is far from the budget, so it is necessary to reorganize again. Considering the difficulties faced by businesses, the Jiangsu Provincial Government will maintain the current tax rate. All districts are now starting to collect the tax. The date for the full implementation of the business tax in Zhenjiang County has been set for August 1st. Those who fail to pay by the deadline will be punished according to the regulations. All businesses must truthfully declare within five days of receiving the declaration form. The Zhenjiang Chamber of Commerce has specially scheduled a meeting for 10:00 AM on the 7th of this month to gather representatives from various industries to discuss the matter.

Police Team Arrests Large Number of Bandits 79

Bu Zhenhai, the captain of the Zhenjiang County Police Brigade, personally led more than 50 police officers from the First Team to Huacun, Xiyingcun, Doujiadu, Mailing, Hongjiacun and other places the night before last at 10:00 PM, and successively arrested 20 bandits. They were immediately taken to the brigade headquarters and transferred to the Security Office for interrogation.

Embankment Collapse at Sangjiawei in Yangzhou's Eight Ports 80

The Sangjiawei embankment in the Eight Ports area under the jurisdiction of the county suddenly collapsed for several zhang (a unit of length) at around 4:00 AM on the 4th. After being discovered, people immediately sounded gongs and gathered a crowd of thousands to rescue it, and the breach was blocked, avoiding disaster.

Husband Falls to Death, Wife Commits Suicide in Qingjiang 81

Wang Pazi, a small boat owner from Shandong, was docked at the Matouzhen in Huaiyin on the inner canal. Pazi tied one end of a rope to his waist and had his wife pull the other end through a pulley at the top of the mast so he could climb up to work. Just as Pazi was leaving the deck and ascending, his wife's pants fell down, so she used her hand to hold them up. As a result, the rope she was holding suddenly gave way, and Pazi fell and died on the boat, his brains splattered. There was no way to save him. His wife, seeing her husband's tragic death, felt so uneasy that she jumped into the water and committed suicide as well. Everyone who heard the story felt saddened.

Bizarre Murder Case at Hangzhou's Hubin Park 82

Yesterday at 3:40 PM, near the wharf of the Second Hubin Park in Hangzhou, A Shui, the 19-year-old son of Qian Xiaoliu, who lived at No. 20, Baijingfang Lane and worked as a peddler, was playfully bantering with his companion Hu Lianshun, 15. This led to a conflict. At first, the two were just wrestling, but Hu Lianshun was knocked to the ground by two slaps to the cheek and died shortly afterward. Qian, realizing he had caused a major disaster, turned and fled. By the time the police arrived, he was gone. The Second Branch sent officers to Qian's house and arrested A Shui's father, Xiaoliu, to take to the station to prepare documents for transfer to the court. The corpse was inspected on the spot by Feng Yongnian, a coroner from the local court's prosecutor's office. Because the cause of death was peculiar, a formal autopsy is required.

Two Bandits Arrested in Hushen Robbery Case 83

The home of Wang Changquan at No. 29, Huian Bridge, Daguan, Hushen, was robbed of gold jewelry, cash, and other items worth over 500 yuan on the evening of the 23rd of last month at around 9:00 PM. At the time, the news was received late, so the bandits could not be intercepted. After looting Wang's home, the bandits crossed the river and hid in Xiaoshan. They were discovered and arrested by the Xiaoshan County Public Security Bureau yesterday. Many beads were found on the spot. Under interrogation, they confessed their names as Ding Xiaosan, "Pockface," 28 years old, from Jiangbei, and admitted to colluding with eight others last month to rob Wang's home in Daguan, Hushen. They also said the ringleader is now hiding in Shanghai. After verifying the confession, the bureau prepared documents and, along with the stolen goods, escorted them to Hangzhou, where they were transferred to the Garrison Headquarters for review.

Impact on the Two Industries After the Abolition of Taels and the Change to Yuan 91

Silver Smelting Industry and Public Valuation Bureau

After the Ministry of Finance Implemented the Abolition of Taels and the Change to Yuan, All Transactions Were Changed to Silver Coins, and Silver Reserves From All Over Were Concentrated in Shanghai, Which Greatly Affected the Business of the Silver Smelting Industry and the Public Valuation Bureau, Which Have a History of Hundreds of Years, After the Abolition of Taels Is Completed, They Will Be Closed Down, According to the Details Obtained by the New Sound News Reporter,

Business Situation of the Silver Smelting Industry 92

The Silver Smelting Industry is a Place for Processing Silver and Casting Treasures, Which Was Founded in the Song Dynasty, Because the Treasures From Other Places Were of Different Fineness, They All Had to Be Recast, Either by Melting Silver Bars or by Recasting Small Foreign Coins, The Silver Smelting Industry Was Entrusted by Banks and Money Shops to Engage in This Recasting Business, If It Was Entrusted by a Bank, the Bank Calculated the Comparison Between Large Silver Bars and Shanghai Ingots, Delivered the Large Bars to the Silver Smelting Industry, and the Silver Smelting Industry Issued a Promissory Note to the Bank as the Silver Smelting Industry's Debt to the Bank, The Procedure Was Equivalent to Discounting a Bill, A Silver Smelting Industry With Good Credit Could Issue a Promissory Note, and a Slightly Less Credible One Had to Have Three Silver Smelting Industries Guarantee Each Other, Limiting One or Two Days After the Ingot Was Cast, It Would Be Delivered to the Bank, If the Bank Entrusted Recasting Treasures From Other Places, the Procedure Was the Same, If the Fineness of the Ingots From Other Places Was Better, the Silver Smelting Industry Still Had to Pay a Discount of Two or Three Taels, If It Was Entrusted by a Money Shop, the Money Shop Estimated How Much the Delivered Ingots or Small Foreign Coins Were Worth in Shanghai Ingots, Agreed With the Silver Smelting Industry, and the Silver Smelting Industry Would Return the Cast Ingots to the Money Shop Within One Day, In Short, the Cast Ingots Had to Be Sent to the Public Valuation Bureau for Approval Before They Could Be Delivered to the Bank or Money Shop,

The Silver Smelting Industry's Organization is the Silver Smelting Guild, Located at the Mouth of Tianhougong Bridge, Henan Road, The Following Are the Most Recent Silver Smelting Industries, Lian Shen, Fuxingli, Beijing Road, Tong Shen, Fuxingli, Beijing Road, Lian Yuan, Fuxingli, Beijing Road, Zhi Qing, Tong Qing, Qingyuanli, Beijing Road, Tong Yuan, Wufuli, Beijing Road, Sheng Tai, Qingyuanli, Beijing Road, Tong Yu, Wan'anli, Beijing Road, Sheng Yuan, Fuxingli, Beijing Road, Tai Heng Yuan, Fuxingli, Beijing Road, Feng Chang, Fushunli, Beijing Road, Tai Sheng, Wufunong, Tianjin Road, Qia Mao, Fushunli, Beijing Road, Hui Tai, Fushunli, Beijing Road, Sheng Xing, Changgengli, Sanyangjing Road,

Inevitably Closed Down 93

Since the Government Ordered the Abolition of Taels and the Change to Yuan, Silver and Ingots Cannot Circulate in the Market, Therefore, the Silver Smelting Industry is Naturally Eliminated, Now That the Abolition of Taels and the Change to Yuan Has Not Been Implemented for Long, Silver From All Over is Being Continuously Transported to Shanghai, Either Delivered to Banks and Money Shops, or Exchanged for Silver Coins, Because the Types of Silver Are Different, Such as Horseshoe-Shaped, Four-Way and Fragmented Silver, Etc., Their Fineness is Inconsistent, Resulting in No Way to Judge, It Must Be Melted Into Ingots by the Silver Smelting Industry and Then Appraised by the Public Valuation Bureau Before It Can Be Exchanged for Silver Coins and Delivered to Banks and Money Shops, If the Abolition of Taels is Successful and Silver Disappears From the Market, Then the Silver Smelting Industry Will Inevitably Be Closed Down at That Time,

Public Valuation Bureau's Public Valuation Method 94

The Shanghai Public Valuation Bureau Was Founded by Wang Lantin From Anhui and is Recognized by Silver and Money Shops, It Has Been Nearly a Hundred Years Since Then, The Address Is at the Intersection of Tianjin Road and Jiangxi Road, The Ingots on the Market Must Be Approved by the Public Valuation Bureau Before They Can Be Used, The Approval Fee is Two Cents and Four Li Per Ingot, If There is Any Smuggling or Omission of Approval, After It Is Found Out, the Approval Fee Will Be Extracted, After the Approved Ingots Are Recalled by Each Family, They Must Be Restored to Their Original Level One by One, If There Is Any Difference in Weight, It Should Be Corrected Immediately, Otherwise the Public Valuation Bureau Will Not Be Responsible, The Public Valuation Method Has Two Types, 1) Weighing, 2) Assessing Fineness, Weighing is Called Managing the Scale, Assessing Fineness is Called Looking at the Fineness, When Doing Public Valuation, First Wipe the Central Concave Part of the Ingot Clean and Hand It Over to the Person Managing the Scale to Weigh It, Then Record Its Weight in the Concave Part With Ink, Then the Person Looking at the Fineness Uses His Eyesight to Judge the Superiority or Inferiority of Its Fineness and Records It in the Central Concave Part, Generally Speaking, the Higher the Fineness, the Approval is Shenshui Two Taels Seven Qian Five Fen, The Lower the Fineness, the Approval is Shenshui Two Taels Six Qian Five Fen, If It Weighs More Than Forty-Nine Taels and Eight Qian, Each Tael is Shen Five Fen, If the Fineness is Below Two Taels and Six Qian Five Fen, It Will Not Be Approved, This Refers to the Ingots Produced by the Shanghai Smelting House, Each Ingot is Standardized at Forty-Nine Taels and Eight Qian, If It Is a Treasure From Various Provinces, Shenshui is Approved According to Common Practice, If It Is a Low-Fineness Treasure, Removing Water to More Than One Tael Will Not Be Approved, If the Person Looking at the Fineness Has Any Doubts, He Can Use a Fangxian Cone to Drill in to Check the Fineness of the Inside, and Then Record It, This Kind of Assessing Fineness Depends Entirely on His Daily Experience,

Temporarily Maintaining the Status Quo 95

After the Abolition of Taels and the Change to Yuan is Implemented, the Silver Smelting Industry is Naturally Eliminated, and the Public Valuation Bureau Was Originally a Public Valuation Business for Ingots Melted by the Silver Smelting Industry, Which is Closely Related to the Silver Smelting Industry, Therefore, Those Who Are Affected Accordingly, If the Silver Smelting Industry is Closed Down, Then the Public Valuation Bureau Will Inevitably Be Unable to Do Public Valuation, But Silver, Which Has Been Used for Hundreds of Years in Our Country's History, Is Either a Habit or Affects the Whole Country, Now Although the Government Has Implemented the Abolition of Taels, It Cannot Be Completely Abolished in One or Two Years, Therefore, It Is Difficult to Realize the Suspension of Business of the Banking Industry, the Smelting Industry and the Public Valuation Bureau for a While, Now All Industries Are Taking Silver to the Central Bank of China, the Bank of Communications and the Bank of China to Exchange for Silver Coins, Which Also Depends on the Public Valuation of the Public Valuation Bureau, Therefore, It Is Said That the Ministry of Finance Will Appoint Talents Familiar With Public Valuation to Supervise the Public Valuation Bureau for Great Faith,

Representatives of National Goods Factories Petitioned in Beijing Yesterday 96

Contributing Opinions on Saving National Goods, Lu Xingzhuang and Others, Standing Committee Members of the Shanghai National Goods Factory Union, Presented a Petition to the Ministry of Industry in Beijing Yesterday, The Original Petition Read, "For the Matter of Requesting Rewards for National Goods Factories in Order to Maintain Industry and Save the Country's Fortune, We Believe That Whether a Country's Industry is Developed or Not is Directly Proportional to Whether the Country is Strong or Not, To Seek National Economic Prosperity, We Rely on the Smooth Sales of National Goods Without Obstruction, Therefore, the Rulers of the Great Powers, in Order to Resist the Dumping of Foreign Goods, Always Protect the Tariff Policy as the Basic Condition for the Development of Domestic Industry and Commerce, It is Undeniable That Our Country's Industry is Backward, In Recent Years, Due to the Global Economic Panic, All Imperialists Are Dumping Their Products Into Our Country, Resulting in an Increasing Annual Trade Deficit, If This Continues, Even Without the Covetousness of Our Eastern Neighbor, We Will Feel Extremely Dangerous, The Government, Aware of This, Has, in Addition to Tariff Autonomy, Also Enacted Anti-Dumping Laws to Prevent the Dumping of Foreign Goods, We Admire Their Foresight, Since the Increase in Tariffs, Foreign Merchants, in Order to Avoid Increased Tariffs, Have All Changed Their Factories to Our Country's Ports, or Increased Capital in Factories That Have Already Been Opened in Our Country in Order to Increase Production, Our Country is Bound by Treaties, We Cannot Prevent Them From Setting Up Factories, Nor Can We Increase Their Tax Rates, Then Chinese Merchant Factories, With Weak Capital, Will Inevitably Be Defeated by Them, If Government Increase the Ex-Factory Tax on All Factories, Regardless of Chinese or Foreign, and Enact Reward Measures to Assist the Development of Domestic Factories, Assuming That Half of the Ex-Factory Tax Collected is Used as a Reward to Be Returned to Domestic Factories, Then, in Fact, the Tax on National Goods Factories is Already Half Less Than That of Foreign Factories, The Cost is Lighter, and Competition is Easier, No Matter How Cunning Foreign Merchants Are, They Cannot Object, This Time, the Government Wants to Issue Bonds of 200,000 Yuan to Rescue Yarn Factories, If It Becomes a Reality, It Will Also Be a Stopgap Measure, It Can Only Help Temporarily, It Is Better to Increase the Ex-Factory Tax and Give Rewards, Which is a Permanent Solution, The Tax on Imported Raw Materials Can Also Be Handled in This Way, It Is a Matter of Maintaining Industry and Can Be Adopted by Your Excellency, We Are Especially Promoted Standing Committee Members Lu Xingzhuang, Ma Jisheng, Zhang Zilian, and Executive Committee Member Jiang Zhonghe as Representatives to Sell Articles and Petition, We Hope That Your Excellency Will Review and Implement It,

The Songhu Garrison Commander Will Be Temporarily Replaced by Chief of Staff Zhang Xiang 101

) Dai Ji departs after the completion of the Memorial Hall (

) The report of his appointment as the commander of the 19th Route Army is unconfirmed (

There have been numerous farewell banquets held by various sectors in recent days, but the date of departure has not yet been determined. Anhui Native Place Association Sends a Letter to the Engineering Department of the National Economic Commission 106

The Magistrate of He County Dismantles the Stone Sluice, Endangering the Riverbank

Representatives from the Two Weirs Come to Shanghai to Beg for Assistance

The Anhui Native Place Association in Shanghai recently received a report from the gentry of He County, stating that the Hekou Stone Sluice, jointly owned by Wu Ran and Zheng Village in the county, had been built by the government to form a complete riverbank and prevent flooding forever. Unexpectedly, the magistrate of He County sent a team to forcibly dismantle it. They requested assistance to protect the livelihoods of the people of the two weirs. The association specifically forwarded a letter to the Engineering Department of the National Economic Commission, stating that according to the letter from Yi Pinshan and others, representatives of the Wu Liang Weir and Zheng Cun Weir in He County, the two weirs, with a circumference of hundreds of miles, are home to tens of thousands of residents and are the richest in the entire county. Between the two weirs is the Lao Xia River, only ten miles away from the Yangtze River. Whenever the river floods, the river flow inundates, and disasters occur when the weir is breached. Magistrate Gao of the thirteenth year of the Republic, after the flood receded, examined the river connecting to the Yangtze River and found that it had more disadvantages than advantages. Therefore, he built a stone sluice at the mouth of the river to open and close it at times. Before the twentieth year of the Republic, there were no floods, which was truly thanks to this. Last year, the National Government repaired the dikes along the Yangtze River and examined the Lao Xia River mouth stone sluice, realizing that there was no need to open it. Therefore, it was strengthened and closed, forming a complete riverbank. The people of the two weirs were all grateful that the floods could be avoided, like the Great Wall. Unexpectedly, a few gentry in Laoqiao Street presented a petition to Magistrate Zhang, ordering him to send a guard team to forcibly demolish the sluice bridge. After the people of the two weirs argued with reason, the demolition was not immediately carried out. More than ten people from the two weirs were taken to the county and detained by the county team, with a deadline of June 20th to demolish it voluntarily, issuing a certificate of guarantee, with severe punishment for violations. Under these circumstances, the people of the weir dared not disobey the order and issued the certificate. However, after the sluice bridge is demolished, the riverbank will be as good as useless. Once the river floods and the raging tide inundates, the weir will break, the fields will be submerged, and the people will become fish. The county magistrate's strict deadline is imminent, and their lives are at stake, so there is no way to do anything. Therefore, they specifically requested your committee to provide assistance, etc. The letter has arrived at the association. The letter states that the Lao Xia River mouth stone sluice is deeply related to the interests of the Wu Liang and Tu Cun weirs. Moreover, when your office repaired the riverbank and closed the stone sluice in the past, it was after thorough investigation and weighing the interests. Now, whether it should be allowed to be demolished or not, your office has its own discretion. In addition to telegraphing the Anhui Provincial Government to order the He County County Government to stop it, it is appropriate to send a letter stating the situation immediately, hoping that you will check and handle it to appease public opinion, and hoping to reply.

Price Dumping to Control Our Fishermen and Fish Merchants

Establishing Companies and Schools for Large-Scale Aggression

According to the Xin Xin News Agency, Japanese fishing aggression has adopted an active policy to oppress fishermen and disrupt the market, which has been seen countless times. The fishing industry has recently received confirmed reports that Japan has further plans, which is to use a price dumping policy to put our fishermen and fish merchants to death. It has secretly ordered its fishing boats to implement two things, namely: 1) to actively engage in fishing in the coastal provinces of China and dump the fish nearby; 2) to equip refrigeration warehouses at various ports in Taiwan, Japan, and on regular shipping routes to sell large quantities of fish products to the coastal provinces and cities of China. In addition, the Japanese government has sent many people to investigate the fisheries of the coastal provinces of our country in great detail, such as the location of fishing grounds, the duration of the fishing season, the quantity of fish caught, the types of aquatic animals, the areas of habitat, and the conditions of migration. Recently, it has even colluded with traitors to organize the Asia Fisheries Company, using its strong capital for planned aggression and to train a large number of aquatic product aggressors, planning to establish a large-scale aquatic product school in Dalian.

Ma Hua and Other Weirs Have Escaped Danger 108

The Engineering Department of the National Economic Commission recently received a report from the Jiangxi-Ganzhou Engineering Bureau that the Xiaolaozhou area of the lower section of the Mahua Dike was in extreme danger due to the collapse of the outer small weir, which caused the Yangtze River waves to directly impact the main dike. With the cooperation of the local people, they did their best to rescue it. Now, the pile driving, soil filling, and the first and second additions of sub-dikes have all been completed, and the danger has been reduced. The third addition of the sub-dike is underway, and strict patrols are being carried out to prevent negligence. In addition, the soil in the Majiawo to Qianjiangkou area of Guangji Weir is sandy and thin. Leakage was found and blocked by pile driving and washing. The inner slope was also strengthened to provide defense. In addition, after the breach of the Xiadacheng Weir in Tongcheng County was blocked and closed, barriers were built and soil was filled on the outer slope, and sack were stacked for protection. The work has been completed, and workers are still stationed there for strict patrols and timely reports to facilitate repairs.

The Tobacco and Alcohol License Tax Sub-Bureau of Shanghai and Baoshan Issues a Notice to Collect Taxes on Liquor and Beer 113

Huang Yong (also known as Yuru), the director of the Tobacco and Alcohol License Tax Collection Sub-Bureau of Jiangsu Shanghai and Baoshan, issued a notice yesterday, stating: According to the report submitted by Ding Xie, the director of the Tobacco and Alcohol License Tax Collection Office, I have been entrusted to handle the collection of tobacco and alcohol license taxes, and I should be responsible for supervising the collection and strive to reorganize it, in order to live up to the intention of seeking truth from facts. I have investigated that Article 3, Item 3 of the Provisional Regulations on Tobacco and Alcohol License Taxes promulgated by the Ministry stipulates that those who simultaneously operate tobacco, alcohol, or foreign alcohol or simultaneously engage in wholesale and retail should obtain licenses separately and pay taxes according to the amount. It is definitely not the case that one alcohol or tobacco license can be used to operate other various types of tobacco and alcohol. The meaning is already very clear. Currently, there are quite a few tobacco and alcohol merchants in Shanghai and Baoshan who simultaneously operate beer, which is a type of foreign alcohol. Most of them have not followed the regulations. This not only violates the Ministry's regulations but also hinders national taxes. At this time when we are trying to reorganize, it is not appropriate to allow them to muddle through. In addition to the director sending personnel to persuade them from house to house, it is now the peak season for beer sales. I would like to ask your bureau to issue a notice quickly, stating that all tobacco and alcohol merchants who also operate beer should obtain licenses separately and pay taxes according to the amount, and submit them to our office for posting separately, so that the public can know. Is this appropriate? I beg you to approve and implement it. According to this, the types of tobacco and alcohol licenses have clear regulations, and alcohol and foreign alcohol must be licensed separately. Now that it is summer, it is the peak season for beer sales, and all tobacco and alcohol merchants and others who also operate beer of this type should obtain licenses separately. It is not appropriate to take advantage of a tobacco or alcohol license. It is related to national taxes. According to the previous situation, in addition to instructing the collection office to conduct a thorough investigation and persuade them properly, if there are any of the above circumstances, they must obtain licenses separately in accordance with the regulations to increase tax revenue. A notice is hereby issued, and all commercial establishments in Shanghai and Baoshan that also operate beer, tobacco, and alcohol must comply and not violate it.

Public Security, Social Affairs, and Public Utilities Bureaus Hold a Meeting to Improve Vehicle Detention Measures 114

Commercial Vehicles Are Generally Not Detained

The XiangSheng Motor Company in this city was previously caught and detained by the Public Security Bureau for transporting contraband goods in its chartered vehicles. The company reported to the Rental Car Association that the driver should be responsible for transporting contraband goods, which has nothing to do with the car. The association sent a letter to the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, requesting that the Public Security Bureau improve the vehicle detention measures. The Public Security Bureau convened a joint meeting of the Social Affairs and Public Utilities Bureaus to discuss the matter in detail and decided on the following measures: 1) Vehicles that violate traffic regulations shall not be detained, except for the vehicle detention measures stipulated in the city's regulations on penalties. The police on duty can record the license plate number and report it for verification. 2) If a driver is careless and causes injury to another person's body or property, the driver should be responsible. In addition to detaining the driver and handling the case according to law, the vehicle should be immediately notified to the owner to retrieve it. However, after a commercial vehicle is registered with the Public Utilities Bureau, it should immediately take out third-party insurance with the Chinese Insurance Company to ensure that the victim can be compensated for the loss. 3) If there is smuggling of contraband goods or serious cases (robbery, kidnapping, murder, reaction), for private vehicles, the driver and the vehicle should be detained and dealt with according to law. For commercial vehicles, in addition to detaining the driver and investigating whether he knew about it and handling it according to law, the vehicle should be immediately notified to the owner to retrieve it. The above measures have been sent by the Public Security Bureau to the Municipal Chamber of Commerce and ordered to all district offices and teams to comply with them.

Citizens of Yinxiang District Oppose Chamber Pot Donation 117

The night soil collectors of the Hujia Muqiao Cleaning Station in Yinxiang District of this city, under the direction of the Seventh District Cleaning Workers' Union, collect a chamber pot donation of five cents per household per month. The collectors are aggressive. The other day, an extortion attempt and assault occurred on an elderly woman surnamed Liu at 3 Lüe Tianfeng Lane, Zhangjiagang. The merchants and residents of the district believe that this trend should not be encouraged, as it may lead to future problems. There is no possibility of accidental extortion fees for cleaning. The local fees that should be paid have been added to the total donation by the municipal government, and other donations and fees shall not be collected privately. The Sanitation Bureau's Order No. 1577 explicitly prohibits the night soil collectors from extorting gratuities. Now, the night soil collectors are actually disobeying orders and using the union as a shield to extort violently from households, causing widespread fear among the people. The citizens held a citizens' meeting at the Hujia Muqiao Fire Station at 2:00 p.m. yesterday, attended by more than 60 representatives from various streets. Zhang Peishen was elected as chairman. The result of the discussion was to unanimously reject this gratuity. A request was also submitted to the municipal government and the Sanitation Bureau for explanation and verification. Ten people, including Zhang Peishen, Teng Zhixiang, Lu Rongguang, and Dai Liming, were elected as the representatives to sign and submit the request. The meeting was adjourned after the discussion.

If he is not satisfied, he will be driven away, forbidden from selling, arbitrarily arrested, punished, and arbitrarily beaten. The victims are countless. We are afraid of the power of the officials and have no choice. Unexpectedly, Patrol Officer Long secretly sent Ma and Yang to repeatedly intimidate and mediate the fees. In order to maintain the livelihood of our families, we endured and paid three or four yuan per stall to make a living. We believe that since you have been in power, all people have relied on protection, and civilians live and work in peace and contentment. How can there be such public officials who abuse their power to extort gratuities, squander money, and disregard the livelihood of civilians? We cannot be at peace. We have no choice but to ask you to investigate and verify and quickly dismiss Patrol Officer Long, punish him with the punishment he deserves, to ensure the livelihood and maintain the law. This is both a public and private virtue. Presented by District Chief Jin."
