)24( Management of Abortion and Premature Birth) A. Abortion and Premature Birth (Abortion after one or two months of pregnancy is mostly discharged unconsciously, without the doctor or midwife noticing. There is also a case where the pregnancy is not yet known, and the person goes out for a trip. Later, the period is suddenly more common, this type; is often a very early abortion.

What is called abortion? It refers to early delivery before seven months of pregnancy, when the fetus still has no ability to live outside the womb. What is called premature birth, means that although the fetus is separated from the mother's womb, it can live, but it has not yet reached the delivery period, it has already been delivered, so it is stable to be a premature birth, according to statistics, the abortion and premature birth of multiparous women is more than that of primiparous women. Now there is a statistical table, based on the amount of findings among 1,226 women, as a comparison is as follows:

)Parous women abortion, Premature birth (Primi parous Women, 131 people 488, Multiparous Women, 241 people 906 people, The easiest time to abort is mostly around three or four months of pregnancy, coming the most, after which it gradually decreases. Abortion in the early stages of pregnancy is actually lightly done by the person unconsciously. As for one month or more and three months or less, then... there is considerable danger, if it is delayed to about five months, then abortion often causes major bleeding, and people suffering from acute avarice or weak heart, there is also the crisis of dying as a result, there is also a so-called incomplete abortion, only the germ cells flow out, all the placenta, etc., still remain in the placenta, which is also a very dangerous thing, which cannot be avoided by a doctor, surgery must be performed first to completely remove it before you can be worry-free.

(B. Omen and Management of Abortion) The omen of abortion, in about a month of pregnancy, flowing down with the period, is unconsciously, without any omen. If you abort in the second or third month of pregnancy, the mucus mixed with blood stains flows down first, after about five or six days or ten days, it is like the air is not smooth, and then suddenly feel back pain, back pain without rest, and then start labor pain, but because of this bleeding, can it be determined to be an abortion? It must be that way. In short; delaying medical treatment is really urgent, if you can do so, you can be spared the worst, and there is also a method of preventing injection.

For the first-aid treatment of abortion, you should lie down quietly on your back, relax your spirit, and place an ice pack on your lower abdomen, use a finger cotton bandage and tape to block the local area, as for the treatment of abortion, it is no different from a normal delivery, but in the points that should be paid attention to, it should be strictly followed. (C. Abortion Should Not Be Ignored) In general, people tend to despise abortion, although it does not greatly harm life in fact, but it is also easy to cause endometritis or substantial inflammation, etc., and it is not a small number of people who become infertile. Also, because part of the placenta and amnion remains in the womb, it causes puerperal fever, or malignant chorionic epithelial tumor, which is a malignant tumor in the womb, resulting in loss of life.

(D. Causes and Prevention of Abortion and Premature Birth) There are many reasons for abortion and premature birth, of which fewer occur due to simple reasons, most of them are caused by a combination of various reasons, so people who are pregnant must have this common sense, so that they can be careful. The main points are described below:

One of the main causes is fetal death, and there are various reasons for fetal death, but no matter what the reason, if the fetus dies one day, it must be discharged from the mother's body.

Pregnant women suffer from infectious diseases such as pneumonia, typhoid fever, cholera, malaria, erysipelas, etc., or have suffered from kidney disease, heart disease, beriberi, pulmonary tuberculosis, leukorrhea, syphilis, etc. Pregnant women have endometritis, substantial inflammation, swelling and sputum, uterine retroflexion, etc.

The location of the placenta is abnormal (that is, placenta previa) Changes such as polyhydramnios, umbilical cord torsion, and twins. Pregnant women suffer from external injuries, that is, due to falls, collisions, disputes, etc., they are stimulated and damaged, or use hot water foot baths, sitz baths, and sea baths, such as long-distance trekking, traveling, boat and car fatigue, abnormal mental emotion, accidental fright, excessive intercourse, etc.

○ Taking medicine during pregnancy is also a cause of abortion and premature birth.

Among the above various causes, such as syphilis, kidney inflammation, uterine retroflexion, endometritis, swelling and sputum, etc., if not completely cured, it is easy to become habitual abortion or habitual premature birth, which will inevitably occur repeatedly, leaving endless troubles and becoming a permanent evil result of infertility.

The prevention method, in addition to first understanding the above various main causes, if the omen of abortion is found, promptly implement the appropriate treatment, then; or this disease can be avoided, this appropriate treatment, in addition to the above-mentioned emergency treatment, should also avoid various exciting foods, and make the spirit and body not fatigued. If you are fortunate enough to turn danger into safety, then; the recuperation afterwards, of course, should be extra careful.

Free Talk

Oblivion 205

— Qi Fan

We have a virtue called oblivion. Oblivion is something everyone and every country has, but we Chinese are particularly good at it, forgetting quickly and cleanly. Whenever unpleasant things happen, while we don't completely ignore them at the time, treating them like fleeting clouds, we can always calmly dismiss them afterwards, as if nothing happened. Even things that aren't so distasteful can be forgotten over time without us even realizing it. For example, officials often forget the blunt advice they gave when they were out of office, young people mostly forget their youthful ambitions, and teachers forget everything they experienced as students.

If we constantly dwell on a pain, always frowning and mourning as if we've lost our parents, wouldn't life become utterly devoid of joy? Moreover, worry can harm us, and if it actually causes illness, wouldn't we be shortening our natural lifespan? Therefore, oblivion is indispensable. Being able to forget allows us to be optimistic, and knowing our fate allows us to settle our lives peacefully. Thus, personal cultivation, family harmony, national governance, and world peace can be established and awaited. The reason China is not yet fully peaceful is probably because oblivion is not yet thorough enough. Furthermore, according to psychologists, people often forget painful and unpleasant things, and the more unpleasant they are, the faster they are forgotten. So, perhaps things in China haven't been terrible enough to make people quickly forget them, preventing us from reaching a state of perfect governance. Thus, there is some indication here on how to bring the nation and society to peace and prosperity, and I believe that current measures and facilities are in line with this grand plan.

There is another meaning to oblivion as a virtue: only by forgetting the old can we accept new ideas. If our minds are full of old, stale, and unpleasant things, how can we accommodate and accept all the new and pleasant things? On the one hand, new events can promote the forgetting of old events. For example, after the May 3rd Jinan Incident, we must forget the May 30th Nanjing Road Incident, and after the September 18th and January 28th Incidents, we must forget the May 3rd Incident. With the loss of Rehe and the North China Armistice Agreement, we must forget that the Northeast was originally Chinese territory. On the other hand, with the hope of winning a 500,000 yuan construction lottery, the losses suffered under the artillery fire in Zhabei must be put out of our minds, and the slogan of cultivating national strength must banish long-term resistance from our memories. I believe that even newer and more pleasant events will emerge, exciting us and making us forget the old entirely, even forgetting that we are Chinese. Oblivion also has a nemesis: the repetition and reminding of events. For example, the May 3rd Incident involved the Japanese, and the September 18th and January 28th Incidents also involved the Japanese. Therefore, the idea that the Japanese are the enemies of the Chinese people cannot be forgotten without prolonged effort. Also, like the civil war, which happens every three months, with fighting resuming every two months, the civil war is deeply hated and resented by the people. The people of Sichuan, for example, must not have forgotten the civil war yet. Chinese people like peace and like to forget, but some people insist on repeating those actions and not allowing people to forget. They are the great enemies of the Chinese people. Those who can bring forth the new through the old are the great talents of governing the country. It is reported that the Barbusse Investigation Group will come to China. I think we have all forgotten the September 18th Incident, and the Lytton Report has become waste paper, but the old man comes from afar to remind us of this unpleasant event. He will surely be opposed by all the people of our country, just like a person in a dream who doesn't like to be called. I think there will always be an event that manifests this, as we indeed have the virtue of oblivion and love this virtue very much, which will surely be fully revealed at that time.

About Zheng Ziyin 206

— A Ying

In Hu Shih's "Fifty Years of Chinese Literature," he once introduced the great poet Zheng Zhen of Guizhou. Zheng Zhen, styled Ziyin, was a native of Zunyi, born in 1806 and died in 1864. He wrote "Nest Sutra Nest Poetry Collection" and other books. Hu Shih said that his collection contained "countless materials for sad poems." Years ago, in Hubei, I was able to borrow the original printed edition of his poetry collection from a friend and selected several poems. At that time, my favorite poems were the nine selected from Volume Three, "Elegy for Second and Third Younger Brothers, Twenty Poems." The poems say:

My ill fate ends here in this life,

Not only a severed hand but also a severed throat.

What can be said about the way of Heaven?

Grief surges like a mountain, but tears do not flow!

The fate of my declining family is pitiful,

No one is as outstanding and virtuous as you.

Even if future generations can be like you,

When the temple is built, the ghosts will be old, and what year will it be?

The rooster crows, calling me to the west side of the house,

A final farewell, only breath remains in your throat.

Eyes point to your three children, entrusting them with a sob,

A lifetime of brotherhood ends in an instant!

Heartbroken that my path grows old and still goes wrong,

How can my limbs be nourished when I am always hungry?

Causing you to suffer in life and suffer in death,

Even in death, you are still clothed in your elder brother's clothes!

I repeatedly planned to travel to Shu, hesitating again and again,

But last month, for no reason, I went and returned again.

I only said that there was a divine intention in our mutual life,

How could I know that it was to see you to your final resting place!

The autumn wind and rain sound mournful,

The pine trees around the mountains were all planted by you.

If even one root does not die, yet my brother dies,

I would cut down everything, not just the ancestral graves.

You served me like a brother, and your wife was like a mother,

Your sister-in-law's heart aches as she tears open her chest.

Most unbearable is the sound of each sob,

I think of all the ways in the world, but none can heal.

My younger brother roared with anger this morning,

His orphaned children fill my eyes, what can I do?

Climbing onto the bed, we all mourn together,

The servants blow the horn and my son plays the zither.

You also reached your life's end at the age of forty-three,

Surely, death is more joyful than a life of poverty.

Thinking that this is not a long-term parting,

I have already become an old man of sixty-nine.

Later, in Shanghai, I bought the "Complete Collection of Poetry and Prose from Nest Sutra Nest," edited and printed by the Ancient Fragrance Huang Family's Ancient Fool Studio. From the various texts in the "Appendix," I learned that his life was extremely miserable. "He suffered from the chaos of the times, the unspeakable hardships of life, wandering and displacement, until his sons were poor and died." In these dozen volumes of poems, there is much tragic historical material from that time, but I only read them hastily and can hardly remember them now. Someday, when I have the time, I would like to read them again and organize this kind of material.

Misfortune 207

— Zhou Lengjia

The wheat has been harvested. After piling all the wheat grains threshed on the threshing ground into the granary, I couldn't help but let out a sigh of relief, as if the burden on my shoulders had lightened a lot.

Walking with a dry tobacco pipe in my mouth, in the soft May evening breeze, I was thinking. My heart was joyful.

"This year's harvest is really not bad! Who would have thought that such rainy weather would produce such a good harvest. If we hadn't lost money on silkworm cocoons, we wouldn't have to worry about making a living for the first half of the year."

I said this to my son. In my heart, I was thinking of many things... Even if this year's wheat price is discounted, it can't escape the price of seven yuan and some change per load. In past years, didn't it sell for more than eight yuan per load? I harvested thirty loads, three sevens are twenty-one, which means I can sell it for two hundred yuan. With this money, not only can I repay Li Laoye's debt with a three-percent interest, but I can also redeem the unlined jacket from the pawnshop. My wife has been complaining about the calico fabric for a long time, and maybe I can even buy some goods for Little Niuzi.

But the next morning, the landlord Chen Daye came to the village in person to collect rent. As soon as he entered the door, he stretched his face and said...

"This year's harvest is good, so I want to collect seven dou of wheat from each mu of land." Seven dou of wheat! I couldn't help but be shocked. Isn't this going to take away half of my family's food and clothing? I could only beg him with a bitter face, asking him to reduce it a bit. My wife also grabbed his clothes and pleaded with him, tears almost falling down.

Chen Daye's heart was truly harder than iron. He turned his face away, snorted, and shouted to the subordinates who came with him to measure the wheat. We were arguing and grabbing, my wife was crying and threatening to hang herself, but it was all useless. The wheat was finally taken away by them! The wheat granary was half empty. Wheat grains were scattered all over the ground. The wheat they took away was at least ten loads.

Several chickens ran over, pecking at the wheat grains on the ground. I kicked them painfully, and they all scattered. One of them squawked strangely and lunged at Little Niuzi's face, scaring Little Niuzi to cry.

Wang Laoda from next door suddenly came over and asked me to go to the city together to ask about the wheat price. I was a little happy again in my heart. There were still twenty loads of wheat left, and as long as the price was the same as in previous years, I could still sell them for one hundred and some change, first pay back the interest on the debt, and then save some... This life can barely be lived.

With such hope, I went to the city. With great difficulty, I walked to the entrance of the Jumi Rice Shop, my heart beating especially hard, and even my arms were trembling a little. I watched Wang Laoda walk to the counter of the rice shop and ask...

"How much is the wheat price selling for?"

"Two and a half yuan."

Two and a half yuan! A thunderbolt struck my ears, and my mind went completely blank. Heavens! What kind of price is this! Am I dreaming? I seemed to see Li Laoye forcing me to pay off the debt, my wife clamoring for calico fabric, Little Niuzi crying for goods, and the unlined jacket pawned in the pawnshop waving before my eyes.

Pearl S. Buck's New Book 208

— Zhao Jingshen

A few days ago, I saw Yi Xian, the translator of "The Good Earth," write an article introducing Pearl S. Buck. Today, I will introduce her new book, "The First Wife," based on The New York Times.

"The First Wife" is a collection of short stories. The story that serves as the title can be said to be a concrete and micro version of her previous novel "East Wind West Wind," again telling the story of a husband influenced by the West and a wife under the old tradition. However, the ending of "East Wind West Wind" is complete, while "The First Wife" is tragic. The husband returns from abroad, and the wife tries her best, but she cannot make her husband happy. He feels that a new life has begun, but she only knows her own world, so she finally commits suicide.

The second short story, "The Old Mother," also tells of the struggle between the old and the new. This story tells of the unhappiness of the old mother. The son is educated abroad and marries a modern girl as his wife. The young couple feels that the old mother's way of life is too outdated, and the old mother also thinks that the two of them are too absurd. "The Day Before" tells of another problem. A young student returns from abroad and finds that his family and relatives are sacrificing their own comfortable lives to increase his status, hoping that he can repay them, but he wants to serve humanity. Should he repay private恩 [ēn, favor/kindness] or serve humanity? He is at a crossroads.

There are also three other short stories... One is about a Westerner's incomprehension of the Chinese, another is Chekhovian, about the unhappy married life of a rural couple, and the last one tells the story of a French petit-bourgeois woman who marries a poor Chinese man and cannot understand his noble character.

There are also several stories under the big topic of "revolution." The first one may be of particular interest to the reader of "The Good Earth," because this is the origin of Wang Long's story. Another one writes about the thoughts of a revolutionary woman in the hours before her execution. "Father Andrea" is the story of a clergyman.

In the last four abridged stories, Pearl S. Buck makes us feel the complex psychology of Chinese farmers resisting floods and famines.

Letter to the Editor 209

To the esteemed Editor:

I read in your publication of July 19th an article by Mr. Wang He, "Talking About the Selection of So-Called Rare Books from the Siku Quanshu," which was relayed to me by a friend.

I am grateful that your publication has published Mr. Wang's concerns about culture and corrections. However, the news reports from various newspapers on the twelfth of last month regarding my talk about the Siku Quanshu were quite inconsistent with the facts, and there were many errors and omissions. I sent a telegram to the Daily News Agency, which published the article, the day after it was reported, raising all the points pointed out by Mr. Wang and asking them to correct them. The news agency was responsible for sending correction letters to various newspapers in Beijing, and many have been published. Although the wording was not detailed, the facts are there for examination. Others may not be aware of this and may have many misunderstandings. Therefore, I drafted this letter in the hope that you will publish it. I am most grateful.

Sincerely,

Jiang Fuzong

Ordinary Matters (34) 210

— Dan Guosun

Zichun's wife, Guanlan, also known as Lao Wu, was such an impatient person. On that entire day of January 28th, she was busy at home, preparing the New Year's Eve dinner. Saying she was "busy" might not be an exaggeration, because the menu for this New Year's Eve dinner was not only elaborate but also complex. The reason for this was to entertain Yao Yongsun. Lao Wu had recently heard Yongsun often talk to Zichun about the fragrant, crisp, and fresh flavors of Fujian cuisine, and she also remembered that Yongsun used to love the crispy, sweet, and exquisite Suzhou boat dishes and pastries. So, as soon as she had arranged for Yongsun to come for the New Year's Eve dinner a few days ago, she had asked someone to find famous chefs from the Suzhou and Fujian schools to come to her home to cook on January 28th, while she herself directed and commanded from the sidelines. Moreover, she was entertaining Yongsun in the manner of entertaining "family," so besides Yongsun, she only invited Yongsun's most trusted retainer, Hong Suiwu, and two young ladies she had met at "Number 281," totaling five people, including herself and her husband.

In the evening, she learned from Zichun that the concession had announced martial law. This inevitably made her a little worried, fearing that Yongsun would not come. Later, she saw that the situation on Chongqing Road outside the door was not panicked, and the night market was still brightly lit, so her heart was half relieved. Soon, the two female guests arrived one after another. They each talked about the situations they had seen outside, and they all concluded that at least in the western district of the concession, everything was the same as usual. However, they were always waiting for the honored guest that day, always anxious but outwardly calm. It was not until about eight o'clock that Yongsun, accompanied by Suiwu, walked in.

This New Year's Eve dinner lasted for more than two hours before it came to an end. Yongsun greatly praised Lao Wu's cooking, and whenever he said a few words of praise, Suiwu would vigorously prove from the side the reasons why it was worthy of praise, so the conversation at the table was also very smooth.

Later, Lao Wu invited them all upstairs to smoke. Zichun chatted with Suiwu and the two female guests, while Lao Wu sat beside Yongsun on the opium couch and prepared the opium for him. In this way, he slowly began to ask about the profits and losses of gambling this year. "This year, I'm probably going to lose about four thousand!" Lao Wu said. "Well," Yongsun said, "that's not a small amount!"

"It's the New Year! I've managed to get by somehow; but after the New Year, I don't have any ideas."

"Ah!" Yongsun sighed in a way that was both intentional and unintentional.

"And what I've managed to get by with somehow still has to be paid back to others!"

"Well, you have to find a way."

"Find a way! Third Master, only you can do it!" As she said this, she raised her head and glanced at Yongsun. "If it were Zichun, he has too few connections."

"That's not so difficult! Slowly... Today is already the twenty-first. I can invite a group of friends to play with you for half a month during the New Year! This way, besides expenses, we can still make a good amount of money!"

"That would be really great! Third Master, thank you so much. But how would we play?" "It's still the old tricks! Fan-tan, pai gow, of course, are indispensable... If the scene is good, we can also have thirty-six doors."

"That would be really great! Third Master, thank you so much. But where would we play?"

Economic Special Publication, Issue 34, Published on Monday

The Quality and Quantity of Raw Cotton Needed in the Future: Zhu Xian Textile 211

Cloth is made from yarn, and yarn is made from cotton. To produce excellent cloth, you must have excellent yarn. To produce excellent yarn, you must have excellent cotton. Therefore, the quality of raw cotton is the main factor in producing excellent yarn and cloth. This is in terms of the quality of the finished product. As for the spinning process, it is even more crucial. If inferior cotton or cotton fibers of non-standard length are used to spin high-count yarn, the amount of waste will increase, the work will be difficult, and production will inevitably decrease. The finished yarn will also be inferior due to insufficient strength. This will affect the weaving process, causing malfunctions, resulting in poor output and inferior fabrics. Therefore, the essential qualities of the raw cotton required for the spinning process, i.e., so-called "excellent cotton," are sevenfold: (1) bright white color, (2) pure and free of impurities, (3) rich in natural twist, (4) fine, long, and soft, (5) uniform length, (6) possessing air space, and (7) adequate strength and elasticity. These have been detailed in my previous work, "The Essential Qualities of Cotton Fibers Required for the Spinning Process." Now, from the standpoint of human progress and industrial rationalization, I will discuss the quality of cotton that our country will need in the future.

(1) The Quality of Cotton Needed for Future Human Progress: As human culture advances daily, material enjoyment also progresses in quality. Clothing is no longer merely for warmth and covering the body but to satisfy desires. Consequently, the demand for coarse, thick cloth decreases daily. Fine cloth, replacing coarse, thick cloth, increases in quantity. The raw cotton for yarn and cloth also gradually becomes finer with the times. Our country's raw cotton has coarse, short fibers that cannot be used to manufacture high-count yarn and fine cloth. To meet the demands of the times, textile factories must spin fine yarn. Inevitably, they must source raw materials from abroad to make up for the deficiency. Below is a classified comparison of the percentage of cotton consumption by yarn factories nationwide in the past four years:

Raw Cotton Consumption Percentages by Year

| Cotton Type | Year 18 | Year 19 | Year 20 | Year 21 |

|---|---|---|---|---|

| Chinese Cotton | 68.25 | 63.11 | 49.67 | 52.13 |

| American Cotton | 13.66 | 13.60 | 26.43 | 38.58 |

| Indian Cotton | 17.99 | 22.76 | 23.29 | 8.81 |

| Egyptian Cotton | 0.04 | 0.21 | 0.31 | 0.03 |

| Other | - | 0.32 | 0.30 | 0.45 |

From the table above, the consumption of Chinese cotton decreased from 68.25% in Year 18 to 38.58% in Year 21. The total consumption of American and Egyptian cotton increased from 13.72% to 39.03%. In Year 20, the total consumption of foreign cotton exceeded that of domestic cotton. In Year 21, it was almost equal. Although this was due to continuous years of famine and poor cotton harvests in the country, the inferior quality of Chinese cotton, which cannot be used to weave fine yarn and cloth, is also a major reason for the decline in consumption. Recently, the consumption of fine, long-fiber American and Egyptian cotton has been increasing daily, while the consumption of coarse, short Chinese and Indian cotton has been decreasing. The situation is becoming increasingly apparent. Factories purchase over 3.5 million piculs of foreign cotton annually, costing over 140 million Customs Taels. The cloth made from this cotton is mostly sold in rural areas. This is equivalent to taking the loss from importing raw cotton and shifting it to the rural areas. On the one hand, the raw cotton produced in rural areas does not meet the demands of textile factories, making it difficult to obtain good prices. On the other hand, the burden of clothing expenses increases, not in proportion to what they produce. As a result, the economy collapses, purchasing power weakens, and the impact on commerce leads to the decline of markets. For industry, it results in unsold inventory. The entire country suffers, unable to extricate itself. Although the decline of our country's economy is due to multiple factors, the lack of production of fine raw cotton has a direct and indirect impact. Therefore, to revitalize the rural economy and supply the textile factories with raw cotton, we must follow the trend of human progress, promote the improvement of raw cotton quality, and meet our own needs. In other words, we must strive to produce fine, long, strong, and white raw cotton. Fine and long fibers can be used to spin high-count yarn. Strength ensures that even high-count yarn has relatively high strength. Whiteness ensures that the finished product is free from defects. These are the essential requirements for producing fine yarn. This is the quality of raw cotton needed in the future from the perspective of human progress.

(2) The Quality of Cotton Needed for Future Industrial Rationalization: The principle of industrial rationalization is to maximize production efficiency with the least amount of machinery and labor. Reducing machinery reduces the initial fixed capital and saves on recurring power, labor, and material consumption. Reducing labor reduces the cost of employing workers. Increasing production reduces the average cost per unit of consumption. This chain reaction leads to lower prices for finished products. Modern textile machinery is also manufactured according to this principle. However, cotton is the only factor that can enable its rationalization. The single-process equipment in the opening room, the "Rieter" and "New Blash" in the carding room, and the high drafting in the spinning room all aim to reduce machinery and maximize production efficiency. However, this is only effective when using relatively clean, long, fine, and strong raw cotton. If the raw cotton is not clean, the fine impurities cannot be completely removed in the cleaning and carding rooms, resulting in defects in the yarn. The drafting action in the roving and spinning rooms will be difficult to perfect. Work will be difficult, output will decrease, and waste will increase. Furthermore, the use of large packages in the roving and spinning machines, the use of multi-spindle winders, and the adoption of automatic devices in weaving machines are all intended to extend doffing and reduce shuttle change times, thereby maximizing efficiency with minimal labor. However, without the use of long, fine, and strong cotton, these effects cannot be achieved. Frequent yarn breaks and frequent machine stops make work difficult, increase labor, and workers cannot endure the tedium, leading to mental exhaustion. This phenomenon is especially pronounced in automatic looms. To achieve automatic efficiency without manual shuttle change, the warp yarn must be resistant to breakage. The ability of the warp yarn to resist breakage depends on the use of cotton with the finest and strongest fibers. In summary, the industrial rationalization of the spinning process depends on the use of raw cotton with clean, long, fine, and strong fibers. This is the quality of raw cotton needed in the future from the perspective of industrial rationalization.

Next, I will discuss the quantity of cotton that our country will need in the future. First, according to the Customs records,

I will list the import values of cotton goods, cotton yarn, and raw cotton since the founding of the Republic, as well as the import volume of cotton, to show the growth and decline of cotton production and imports in our country over the past twenty years.

| Year | Cotton Goods (Customs Taels) | Cotton Yarn (Customs Taels) | Raw Cotton (Customs Taels) | Raw Cotton (Piculs) |

|---|---|---|---|---|

| Year 1 | 84,927,866 | 63,352,860 | 4,929,402 | 2,793,56 |

| Year 2 | 133,369,801 | 72,946,905 | 31,262,211 | 1,289,35 |

| Year 3 | 127,163,276 | 67,433,544 | 34,404,031 | 333,87 |

| Year 4 | 228,738,616 | 68,572,180 | 70,416,693 | 363,322 |

| Year 5 | 752,522,516 | 64,253,446 | 84,560,654 | 407,225 |

| Year 6 | 970,247,606 | 68,544,986 | 67,149,812 | 99,850 |

| Year 7 | 1,001,783,075 | 59,146,116 | 163,308,841 | 189,990 |

| Year 8 | 1,419,802,679 | 134,082,687 | 6,870,674 | 239,218 |

| Year 9 | 1,708,642,798 | 84,507,676 | 184,767,266 | 686,373 |

| Year 10 | 1,457,014,797 | 72,158,170 | 362,731,901 | 1,704,060 |

| Year 11 | 1,541,240,267 | 71,229,571 | 439,872,501 | 1,780,618 |

| Year 12 | 1,328,711,374 | 44,178,897 | 546,504,316 | 1,614,371 |

| Year 13 | 1,544,710,493 | 36,867,638 | 498,368,951 | 1,241,881 |

| Year 14 | 1,520,155,204 | 41,353,981 | 708,525,081 | 1,807,450 |

| Year 15 | 1,721,222,331 | 31,163,048 | 954,738,102 | 2,745,017 |

| Year 16 | 1,317,825,161 | 19,899,614 | 822,042,722 | 2,415,482 |

| Year 17 | 1,665,812,151 | 19,222,867 | 685,487,781 | 1,916,140 |

| Year 18 | 1,674,604,961 | 16,619,289 | 207,810,525 | 2,514,786 |

| Year 19 | 1,328,862,671 | 12,778,344 | 1,332,345,673 | 4,564,940 |

| Year 20 | 1,071,653,474 | 4,091,850 | 1,798,224,646 | 4,652,726 |

| Year 21 | 725,742,589 | 3,579,752 | 1,288,566,153 | 3,712,856 |

From the table above, the import of cotton goods gradually increased after Year 7. The import of cotton yarn was higher before Year 11 and gradually decreased after Year 11. The import of raw cotton was minimal before Year 8 and gradually increased afterward. In Year 20, it reached a high of over 4.6 million piculs, with a value of over 170 million Customs Taels, ranking first among imported goods. This indicates that the domestic supply of raw cotton is insufficient and the quality is not suitable for use. In summary, over the past twenty years, the people of our country have worked hard on the textile industry and made considerable progress. Therefore, the import of cotton yarn has been reduced to a minimum. The import of cotton goods in the last three years has not been as high as it was between Year 8 and Year 18. However, the increase in the import of raw cotton has exceeded the decrease in the import of cotton yarn and cotton goods. The gains from the efforts of the textile industry are not enough to offset the losses from the increased import of raw cotton. The total value of cotton imports has not been reduced. How can the rural economy avoid collapse? How can the national strength avoid daily decline? Cotton farmers do not know how to improve cotton production, and the government does not pay attention to cotton farmers, allowing them to fend for themselves, leading to today's consequences. The opportunity for recovery begins now. Regarding the quantity of cotton needed in the future, I will address those who are dedicated to promoting cotton value.

Our country currently has over 4.5 million spindles. Over 2.5 million spindles are owned by Chinese businesses, while over 2 million spindles are operated by foreign merchants. The annual consumption of cotton is over 8.9 million piculs. Domestic cotton production is over 8 million piculs. After deducting the cotton used for clothing, bedding, and a small portion used in the hand-weaving industry, only about 5 million piculs are available for supply to spinning mills. Therefore, there is still a shortfall of over 3 million piculs, which must be sourced from foreign cotton. However, the current number of spindles is far from being able to be self-sufficient. Even the current cotton production is far from being able to be self-sufficient. Cotton production must be actively increased. Please refer to the development status of the domestic textile industry and promote it in two phases.

The first phase aims to meet the consumption needs of the existing spindles. In addition to the existing production, we must vigorously increase the planting of fine, long, strong, and white cotton: 1.3 million piculs of cotton with a length of 3/4 inch to 1 inch, 3.4 million piculs of cotton with a length of 1 1/16 inch to 1 3/16 inches, and 600,000 piculs of cotton with a length of 1 1/4 inch to 1 1/2 inches. A total increase of 5.3 million piculs is required.

The second phase, according to my work "The Three-Three Plan for Promoting the Cotton Industry," involves increasing spindles by 4.05 million and looms by 97,300. The yarn produced by the spindles can meet the weaving needs of the looms. The cloth produced by the looms can meet the clothing and bedding needs of the entire country. The increase in cotton production must adapt to the consumption of these spindles: 10.1 million piculs of cotton with a length of 3/4 inch to 1 inch, 4.7 million piculs of cotton with a length of 1 1/16 inch to 1 3/16 inches, and 1 million piculs of cotton with a length of 1 1/4 inch to 1 1/2 inches or more. A total of 15.1 million piculs is required.

The above only discusses the quantity of cotton that needs to be increased in the future. As for how to increase cotton fields, how to improve cotton seeds using scientific methods, and how to guide cotton farmers to improve cotton cultivation, these are agricultural matters. At this time when rural areas urgently need to be revitalized and the quality and quantity of raw cotton urgently need to be improved, I hope that those responsible for improving cotton production will recognize the importance of their mission, fulfill their duties, and benefit our rural areas. Supply our textile industry with the raw cotton it needs and stop relying on foreign cotton imports, which will sever our national lifeline. Our textile industry must provide economic cooperation to the cotton industry. Good quality raw cotton should be given a reasonable price to stimulate cotton farmers' interest in improving cotton quality. If producers and consumers work together to increase the quality and quantity of cotton, it will not be difficult to achieve final success. This is what I sincerely hope for.

The Most Serious Currency Problem in the Current Stage of World Economic Panic: Huang Zhang 212

The current stage of world economic panic is the most serious ailment afflicting capitalism today. The doctors have gathered once again, including politicians, theorists, practitioners, industrialists, financial experts, and wealthy merchants from various countries. It is truly a magnificent gathering! This is the London World Economic Conference, which opened on June 12 and recently adjourned. These doctors, each with their own remedies, engaged in eloquent debates at the conference. However, they ultimately failed to reach a consensus on a common remedy. The moribund patient, capitalism, continues to writhe in agony on its sickbed. How tragic! What is this intractable ailment? Let us analyze it in detail.

I. Rigid Tariff Barriers 213

The current situation, while not hopeless, is certainly serious. This economic ailment is none other than what doctors call "arteriosclerosis." In the major capitalist countries, production figures have decreased by two-fifths compared to 1929. Since last fall, the decline in production figures has stopped, but international trade figures have shown a downward trend. The total volume of world trade in the first three months of 1933 was only 35% of the total volume in the same period of 1929, and even lower than the same period of 1932. The circulation of goods is becoming increasingly difficult, and the major arteries of world trade are becoming more and more stagnant. The economic blood, the goods, is not circulating sufficiently in the blood vessels. This is an undeniable fact.

The so-called "arteriosclerosis" of modern capitalism, in economic terms, is "protectionist madness." The closure of borders in various countries has become even more severe in 1933. According to the recent research by the Economic Research Group of the League of Nations, the Industrial Daily News has listed some of the major serious issues as follows:

"From the perspective of tariffs, we can say that since January 1933, the revisions of tariff laws in various countries have been countless. These revisions, instead of alleviating the current ailment, have aggravated it.

Sweden, Norway, Czechoslovakia, Poland, Switzerland, Hungary, the United Kingdom, and others have all revised their tariff laws. Germany's increased taxes on livestock and fresh meat have de facto violated certain tariffs stipulated in the commercial treaty signed with France in 1927. Similarly, France, in order to restore its commercial balance with Germany, has also restricted the import of many German goods.

We can also cite the example of Austria, which converted the British gold coins payable as tariffs into schillings. In this conversion, it de facto increased the tax rate by 25%.

France has also increased the so-called 'exchange compensation' additional tax levied on imports from China, Japan, Ceylon, New Zealand, South Africa, and the Soviet Union. Based on these tariff changes, the commercial situation in various countries has had to be reorganized. Everywhere, foreign imports are restricted, and the methods of restriction are being strengthened daily. Because countries are finding other ways to develop various abnormal forms of commerce, France has had to restrict the import of new goods. The same is true for Switzerland, Austria, and Hungary. The economic instability of all countries is naturally reflected in their treaty policies."

Since last fall, the phenomenon of declining production has stopped, which seems to indicate that the current economic situation is somewhat better than a year ago. Today's pain and suffering stem from the fact that after expanding production, we encounter severe tariff wars in various countries, which stiffen the arteries of international commerce, making it impossible for this huge volume of goods to circulate in the international market. If we want to activate the production sector, the only way is for countries to implement a tariff truce! However, in a time when countries want to maintain commercial balance, is a tariff truce possible?

The world economic situation in the three and a half years since the explosion on Wall Street can be summarized as follows: From the perspective of production planning, the panic of oversupply continues to subside, but the ailment of stagnation has taken its place. In most industrial sectors, there is no longer a phenomenon of overproduction. Supply no longer exceeds demand. In fact, supply has been greatly reduced, while demand has increased. The imbalance between production and purchasing power, which caused the panic, has been reduced. Naturally, in a mechanized capitalist society, production either advances or retreats. Since demand has relatively increased and the imbalance between production and purchasing power has been eliminated, the production of various goods has increased. However, unfortunately, just as the possibility of developing production plans arises, serious obstacles occur in the circulation plans: the firm and high tariff barriers, the restrictions on various imported goods, and the bans on the entry of various imported goods seem to completely obstruct international trade. This is a very obvious ailment in the current stage of the world economic panic.

II. Currency Chaos 214

There are two main reasons why international trade is so stagnant. First, some capitalist countries, seeing that the number of their goods sold in foreign markets has greatly decreased, have had to regard their domestic markets as forbidden zones, refusing the import of foreign goods. The economic panic of recent years has pushed this trend to the extreme. Second, the panic of recent years has put the fiscal budgets and banking plans of various countries in a very volatile state, so that the stability of currencies is greatly threatened. Because of the volatility of currency prices, not only have the existing restrictions of various countries become more severe, but also new restrictions are being promulgated in batches. There are two types of these restrictions: Direct restrictions are imposed because some countries' currency situations are already in danger, and they must maintain a minimum amount of gold as a reserve, prohibiting the export of gold. In this way, they de facto lose the ability to purchase goods from abroad. Indirectly, some countries' currencies are stable, but in order to resist the currency hoarding policies of countries with depreciated currencies, they have to adopt protective measures.

Many countries want to maintain the gold standard, and some countries want to abandon the gold standard, but in many cases, the same unfortunate result occurs.

The United Kingdom and the United States, not to mention their protectorates and colonies, have made the chaos in the world market more serious since abandoning the gold standard. On the one hand, they prohibit the free circulation of gold, and on the other hand, they have aroused the protective policies and countermeasures of various countries regarding gold.

In order to maintain currency stability and to maintain the integrity of gold reserves, Germany and most of the Central and Eastern European countries have had to issue many regulations to prevent the import of foreign goods. Naturally, those countries that are thus harmed will also find ways to retaliate.

Therefore, we can say that in the current stage of economic panic, the currency problem is very serious. The international trade market is so depressed, and countries are mutually bound by tariff restrictions. It is clear that we cannot say that after the currency problem is properly resolved, the tide of protectionism can be curbed, and all the tariff barriers that resemble the Great Wall of China can be broken! Besides currency instability, there are other reasons for this protectionism, namely the narrow and monopolistic nature of commodity outlets (such as cartels and syndicates). This is no less important than currency instability! But who will pay attention to this difficult and rigid problem, a problem that is the inevitable trend of capitalism?

This is why the London World Economic Conference specially discussed the currency problem. The opposition between France and the United States and the repeated suspensions of the conference were all due to this currency problem.

Three. The Ideal and Reality of Solving the Currency Problem 215

We know that there is currently a most significant problem in the world, from which the disarmament conference, the Lausanne Conference, and the London Economic Conference all originated; this is the long-unresolved war debt problem. Because the United States opposed discussing this issue at the London Economic Conference, the preparatory committee for the London Conference did not include it on the agenda. Although MacDonald tried his best to propose discussing this issue at the general assembly, it ultimately yielded no results due to the passive resistance of the U.S. representative Hull, who refused to attend. Since the war debt problem remains unresolved, the debtor nations have no choice but to pay cash to the United States, causing their reserves to dwindle day by day, which in turn causes fluctuations in currency values. Without resolving the fundamental war debt problem and merely engaging in peripheral issues such as currency values and opening exchange rates, it is naturally difficult to achieve any results. The failure of the London Conference to achieve any significant results was expected long ago.

It is not enough for us to simply recognize the importance of the currency problem; it is also not enough for us to simply agree that it is necessary to find a way to solve this currency problem. We must know: First, why and in what sense is this currency problem the most important issue in the current stage of the economic panic? Second, how can this problem be solved in any way? Third, if a proper solution is obtained, what methods can we use to make the relevant countries implement it?

Regarding the first question, there are naturally many different opinions. Some economists say that the instability of currency is one of the causes of the world's economic panic. They imagine that the panic occurred because prices have fallen. Such a simplistic observation is no different from saying that the weather is bad because the barometer is indicating rainy weather! The general vulgar economists say that to alleviate the panic, we only need to raise prices. Isn't that like saying that to make the weather clear, we should quickly adjust the rain/sun indicator on the barometer! Such a theory is truly absurd!

Other economists pay more attention to the facts. They believe that the currency problem is not responsible for the economic panic. In other words, the panic is not due to the decline in currency values. Solving the currency problem will not guarantee future prosperity. However, they believe that countries should also find ways to ease their separate protectionist measures because easing protectionist measures would allow capital to flow freely, and industry and commerce could slowly recover. This has considerable merit.

Is the currency problem truly the root of all panics? Are currency fluctuations and price fluctuations truly the cause of the current economic disaster? Or, although the currency problem is not related to the revival of the world's industries, does it still remain a major issue in the current stage of the panic? All of these questions are subject to different opinions and perspectives. For example, the U.S. representative said that the currency problem is not important, and the devaluation of the U.S. dollar is an urgent measure to raise prices, restore people's purchasing power, and revive industry and commerce, which is beneficial to all countries. However, France is in a completely opposite position. She believes that without stabilizing currency values, no international cooperation can begin. These are naturally statements made from the standpoint of national interests, which is not surprising. So, if economists from all countries speak from the standpoint of their national interests, how can a unified view be obtained!

Based on different views on the first question, naturally, there will also be different opinions on the second question: how can this currency problem be solved? Fundamentally speaking, if the United States is unwilling to resolve the war debt problem, then all solutions to the currency problem will still be problems. Even leaving aside the war debt problem, what methods can we use to make the currencies of various countries achieve relatively consistent values? What kind of exchange rate should be used to stabilize the exchange rates of various countries? Is it possible to have countries with different interests in producing, storing, and using gold, as well as producing, storing, and using silver, jointly construct an international currency standard? All of these contradictions cannot be resolved in a selfish and self-serving capitalist world. It is not at all surprising that the London Conference could not reach a unified conclusion.

Regarding the third question, if we obtain a proper solution, what methods can we use to make the relevant countries implement it? This is very obvious. International conferences are not uncommon in history. The result of the conferences is always the emergence of some grand resolutions, but once the conference is over, everyone still acts according to their own interests, regarding the resolutions as mere words. How often have we seen the fact of abiding by covenants!

Therefore, although the currency problem is a most serious problem in the current stage of the panic, it is not a fundamental problem. Even if the London Conference continues to meet and obtain some temporary measures to stabilize currencies, it will ultimately not solve the world's economic panic. This is because there is no way to eliminate the selfish and self-serving economic systems of various countries, and there is no way to eliminate the economic contradictions between countries. Moreover, the war debt problem after the European war continues to intensify the antagonism between Europe and the United States! (Drafted on July 27, 1933.)

Securities Sellers Repeatedly Showed Their Strength 218

The bond market weakened throughout the past week. From July 31st to August 5th, the Shanghai Chinese Securities Exchange saw a slight decline in the market due to the market conditions offering an opportunity for short-selling speculation. The situation, such as Feng's stubbornness and the central government's intention for peace, had not yet been realized. The Japanese were also taking threatening actions in North China and engaging in various forms of coercion and sabotage against the League of Nations' technical cooperation. All of this news was unfavorable to the bulls. This was just the surface situation. In fact, since the market prices had soared on July 19th, most contracts were already around 65% of par value. The 18 series and 19 series customs bonds were already above 78% of par value. At this time, it was actually awakening the shorts' desire to observe. However, because of short covering before the settlement of the July futures contracts, the prices were still fluctuating. After the July 28th settlement, Feng's army remained stubborn, and the rumors in North China intensified. The shorts became bolder. Various groups and the North Group sold off every day, causing the market prices to struggle but ultimately fail to rally due to the severe oppression of the shorts. The market gradually declined day by day. On Monday, the central government issued a telegram calling for peace, but Feng's army had not yet responded. News of the loss of Duolun emerged, and short selling surged. The market prices fell by a small amount of 7-8 jiao. On Tuesday, the North Group had another large-scale fire sale, and the market still failed to recover. On Wednesday, large players and the North Group continued to sell, and the bulls also emerged, causing another decline of 7-8 jiao. On Thursday, the North Group continued to sell, but the large players showed no interest, continuing the small decline of 3-4 jiao to 7-8 jiao. On Friday, although the North Group had stopped selling, the bulls and retail investors emerged and sold short, causing the market to continue to decline, even more severely than before, with declines ranging from several jiao to over two yuan. In total, the market fell for six consecutive days until Friday. The market conditions were indeed unfavorable to the bulls, but in reality, it was still due to the fierce and repeated suppression by the sellers, which caused the bulls to wait and see to prevent organized short selling. On Saturday, the situation suddenly took a sharp turn for the worse. The bulls seized the opportunity to retaliate, and the shorts were defeated. Therefore, the shorts initially wanted to suppress the market to a small extent, but ultimately, because people's confidence had already increased, the market prices turned sharply higher, recovering several jiao to 1.6-1.7 yuan. At this time, the North Group's shorts were still waiting and seeing. The future trend is still subject to many changes. As a result of the week's market prices, there was a total decline ranging from several jiao to two yuan. The trading volume was also quite active, with a total turnover of 61,009,500 yuan, including 69,500 yuan in spot transactions and 60,094,000 yuan in futures transactions.

Talks

Where Exactly is the Way Out? 223

In this everything is contradictory and deformed society, it is inevitable to reflect the accumulated contradictions. Therefore, things like "getting rich quick," "horse racing tickets," and "lottery tickets" should also be products of a contradictory society, you see. Many people grasp at anything in the more contradictory it is. It is clear that the hope of buying any lottery ticket is as illusory as trying to find a needle in the ocean, but a group of people, of course, with poor folks accounting for the vast majority, are unwilling to give up this faint hope. Every time I see people being so enthusiastic, I simply don't believe that society is in decline. To speculate about the reason for such contradictions, the answer is probably: "There is no hope that can be better than the hope offered by this kind of illusion in this real society."

You might think that this kind of hope is an expression of extreme individualism? Correct. They spend their hard-earned money, even a few cents extracted from hunger, to make this desperate gamble, which is undoubtedly because they have a great desire to get rich. But on the other hand, there is also a point that is equally worthy of our attention, which is that they want to avenge the dissatisfaction that reality has dealt them, and they also place this attempt at revenge on this illusory hope. Isn't this the secondary condition that pushes them into the hope of destruction?

Isn't that right? I have several friends who bought this "XX lottery ticket." Before the lottery was drawn, they were already preparing to distribute that astonishing sum of ten thousand yuan. One of them wanted to get a few gorgeous women to play with because his wife had run away with a certain young master when he was desperately poor. Another wanted to buy several cars to rush and crash on the streets as a demonstration because he was tired of being bullied by the arrogant cars on the road every day. In short, they hate reality and want to plant some seeds of revenge in the hope of illusion. Very few of them held the idea of settling down and building a career peacefully. It's just a pity that none of my friends won the prize. Such passive expressions are indeed laughably naive.

Of course, apart from the lucky one who gets the sole prize money, there must be millions who are disappointed and sad. But someone said: "We were so happy before the lottery was drawn, dreaming sweet and dense dreams! Although this dream is somewhat empty and illusory, having this kind of empty dream on this tired and mechanical mind all day long is already the supreme glory and comfort." When we ask ourselves whether this kind of Ah Q thinking is right, of course, this kind of "temporary beautiful dream" hope is not a way out either! Because, does the money they exchange with blood and sweat only worth this little price? No, definitely not, then what is our way out?

Doing a good job as someone, accumulating some money bit by bit is the best way out, right? But simply put: in today's society, wanting to accumulate some money is a dream. You are already a lucky person if you can solve the problem of three meals a day. Then what is our way out?

The above two paths are already impassable, so we should find a third path! Let's assume that the above two paths are "dream paths," then the one we want to take now must be "in sobriety." "Sober path" definitely cannot be lying in bed, it should be soberly getting up to find a way out. But after all, it is also a difficult thing! It is like sharp thorns are placed in front of your bed, making you unable to get up. If you sleep down again, it is full of mud, and it will be difficult for you to get up again. Then what is our way out?

But mankind always runs towards the path of survival!

The Inside Story of Hiring Teachers 225

— Ba Yi

In the small advertisements in the newspapers, there are often notices for hiring teachers, especially in the summer during the summer vacation, because the summer vacation is the time for various schools to replace teachers. The psychology of unemployed people is depressed. They feel the sorrow and pain of unemployment, so they desperately look for things to do. Therefore, the recruitment category in these classified advertisements has become a daily necessity for the unemployed. My friend Mr. K was naturally no exception.

One summer evening, I was enjoying the cool in the courtyard when I suddenly heard a burst of very hurried footsteps coming straight towards my house. I looked closely and saw that it was Mr. K. He saw me and said, "There is now an opportunity to be a teacher! This opportunity is what I found in the newspaper, look!" I took the newspaper and looked at it. There was a passage like this:

Our school now plans to hire six teachers. Qualifications: must be a teacher training school graduate. Salary: 30 yuan per month, with room and board provided. Those who are willing to apply should bring their certificates and a registration fee of two yuan to XX Road XX Lane XX Number for contact and registration, and wait for an interview. Those who are suitable will be hired. School.

After reading it, I said to Mr. K, "Although this is an opportunity, you have to be careful. Is it reliable? Don't be slippery? What about the inside story?"

After hearing my words, K said, "I don't care whether they are slippery or not, whether there is an inside story or not. I have been unemployed for a long time. How can I sacrifice this opportunity? Anyway, the registration only costs two yuan. If it's an inside story, then I can only admit that I'm unlucky, like having a disease, right?"

After K finished speaking, he left slightly. After a week, K came again. Seeing his appearance, he was very depressed, not as lively as before. Before I had time to ask him, he said first, "Old friend, I've been tricked! That time's teacher recruitment was indeed an inside story! Slippery! This time when I went to register, a young man in a suit was working in this room. At this time, there were already more than 100 people registered. I also registered according to the law. After two hours, the man in the suit asked me about my resume and hometown, etc. Finally, he said, 'I will notify you after three days.' So I paid two yuan and went back.

After I got home, I waited all day long for the notification. Unexpectedly, after three days, there was no notification. I couldn't help but be suspicious, so I hurriedly went to the registration office to find out what was going on. It was already empty, according to the neighbors, they had moved out the day before yesterday. Old friend, isn't this an inside story? Slippery? I have really been tricked badly."

After listening to his words, I couldn't help but be stunned. I thought silently that it is really difficult for young people to enter the world in this society that is full of darkness and miasma. There are countless traps set up in advance, waiting for young people to step into them, which is really extremely dangerous! Mr. K's deception is still a small matter. However, the bankruptcy of education can also be seen from this. Alas, alas, alas.

Announcements 227

Yu, Wu, Ping, Qiling, Shenmin, Yao, Jianyin, Yi, Jiexin, Liangyi, Xiang, Lijuan, Mang, Liehuo, Houying, Baling, Chang, Chen Ruidian, Jack, Guanghan, Xiangyun, Bing, Mengfei, Xiaozhi, Xian, Zao, Yiping, Xuyu, Xizhang, Chengming, Hu, Peishan, Xue’an, Liangfeng, gentlemen, please note that the royalties for the month of July have now been settled. Please bring your seal and a receipt to the accounting department to collect your payment from the 6th to the 10th of this month, and from the 16th to the 20th of this month.

Binfu, Huan Yixi Lin, Wen, Jinzhi, Pengnian, Xueying, Tianlong, Yin Chengyu, Bu Denglong, Chang, Xing, Yu, Xiyuan, Liang, Luoyang Shaonian, Lin Ru, Erchu, Xiaohong, Dongliang, Qizhi, Yan, Zhengping, Cheng Ding, Zhongpo, Yan, Wenjun, Yizhang, Huicheng, Wufi, Wenjie, gentlemen, please send a supplementary seal and letter of certification within three days in order to settle your accounts.

Regarding the illustrations "Unsanitary Rickshaw Pullers" published on July 4th, "Commonplace Music in the City" published on July 6th, "Deformed Development" published on July 11th, "Capitalists and Labor" published on July 11th, and "Four Ages of Women" published on July 12th, the original manuscripts were lost during plate-making, making it impossible to verify the signature and seal. Artists who drew the above five illustrations, please send a letter of certification with your seal within one week to receive payment, and please attach a recent drawing for comparison of style. Signed, Editorial Department of the Shanghai Supplement.

Fiction

Under the Traffic Lights (46) 228

— Xilin

(25) "Wavy hair is fine as long as the heart is upright and true. This might give our dull commerce and industry some new stimulus! Good." Wu Ziqing was ultimately more experienced than them, pressing the question deeper: "However, the attitude we adopt externally must be very cautious. Tomorrow, I think… Currently, there are already some rumors about our attitude externally. I think it would be good to have a statement issued by the banking community tomorrow denying everything!"

"Alright!" Yang Jiefu breathed a sigh of relief. "Yishan, let's arrange a tea dance party at your place the day after tomorrow. Let's get some of our colleagues together to sound out their opinions."

It was only ten o'clock, and each of them had plenty of time to pick his favorite concubine and enjoy the second half of the night for an hour or two.

Wang Hua was too much in the limelight. Now he went to every meeting, and whenever he did, he would speak, and whenever he spoke, he would talk about saving the country, and whenever he saved the country, it was always greatly beneficial to him.

Everyone said Wang Hua was an active member, a capable man, but everyone despised his lack of knowledge and his base character. He became the subject of conversation for many people, which he took as a source of honor. He believed that being qualified to be talked about proved that he was not born silent and odorless, and even if someone scolded him, it was just jealousy. But no one dared to offend him, and that was something he could certainly be proud of. Wasn't it true that no one had ever exposed the many dark deeds he had done? Here, there was yet another one of them. Ever since he had Professor Li rope in a group of famous Shanghai celebrities to collect donations for national salvation, he had indeed received a thousand responses to his call, gathering fur (?), to make a robe. But this fur was torn from the bodies of poor people. Some reduced their meals, going hungry to save a few dimes, some lengthened their working hours to earn a few extra cents, women specially knitted a pair of socks as a donation, and even children would save their candy money to donate. Their achievements were wildly praised in the newspapers, as if they were about to lead a national mobilization of the people. In order to encourage the people to continue to donate, they often held large-scale gatherings to celebrate the generals of the Northeast Anti-Japanese Volunteer Army. One day, it was reported that a representative of a certain Northeast Volunteer Army had come to Shanghai to seek assistance, and would attend a reception hosted by the Anti-X X X X Organizations Joint Association to report on the anti-Japanese situation. The name of this representative X X X X sounded unfamiliar, but most of the generals and soldiers of the Northeast Volunteer Army were grassroots heroes who rose up spontaneously, and it was common for their names to be unknown to the people of the country. As long as they raised the banner of resistance against Japan, their compatriots would sympathize with them unconditionally. Therefore, the reception held by the X X X X Organizations Joint Association was very popular, with many eager to participate. Hu Yuan announced the opening of the meeting, followed by the chairman I the chairman was of course our hard-working Brother Hua eating I introducing the resume of the said Volunteer Army representative.
